
Processing Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment claims in Process Direct 003-22011652

-   Background
-   Process
-   References
-   Resources
-   Training & Support

[Expand/Collapse all sections]Expand all

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

If allocated an online claim or Assisted Customer Claim, do not process
it in Customer First. If staff are allocated one and not trained in
processing in Process Direct, they should speak with their team leader
or Service Support Officer (SSO) for help reallocating the work item.

Customers can claim online again from 8am Wednesday 20 July 2022. If a
customer calls, tell them to visit
https://www.servicesaustralia.gov.au/pandemic-leave-disaster-payment for
how to claim online. If a customer does not have access to online
services, they can claim over the phone using Assisted Customer Claim
(ACC) from 9am on the same date.

There are different claiming periods depending on the self-isolation,
quarantine or caring period claimed. See the Resources page.

If a customer has lodged a claim online or using ACC that has not yet
been finalised, they cannot lodge another one. If a customer calls to
ask why they cannot lodge more than one claim, tell them:
‘You can lodge your next claim once you have received confirmation from
Services Australia on the claim outcome of your previous claim.’

Reminder: more than one Flexible Support Payment (including Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment) cannot be paid on the same day. See Processing
Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment claims in Process Direct.

This page has information to help staff process Pandemic Leave Disaster
Payment claims from 18 January 2022 in Process Direct.

Always assess a customer's eligibility for payment by also referring to
Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment.

On this page:

Review claim

Rejecting claims

Asking for information or evidence

Escalating claims

Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment was incorrectly paid

!FFAP Screen - processing claims

Fifth or subsequent claim – request evidence

Reporting potential fraud

Cancelled JobSeeker Payment or Youth Allowance

POIPLDP manual review allocated

Review claim

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

|                                   | Withdrawal confirmed              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   has submitted the same        |
|                                   |     information in each claim and |
|                                   |     has not previously been       |
|                                   |     requested to provide evidence |
|                                   |     to support their claim, keep  |
|                                   |     assessing the claim           |
|                                   | -   made minimal changes and they |
|                                   |     are advising the same         |
|                                   |     circumstances for this ACC,   |
|                                   |     it is reasonable the customer |
|                                   |     may have had issues with the  |
|                                   |     claiming process. For         |
|                                   |     example, number of hours      |
|                                   |     lost, or self-isolation,      |
|                                   |     quarantine or caring dates    |
|                                   |     for overlapping periods. Keep |
|                                   |     assessing the claim           |
|                                   | -   tried to change responses to  |
|                                   |     the questions in each claim   |
|                                   |     submitted and when lodging    |

|                                   |     assessing all other criteria, |
|                                   |     to discuss why responses have |
|                                   |     been changed. Keep assessing  |
|                                   |     the claim.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the customer is      |
|                                   | showing behaviour that may        |
|                                   | suggest their claim is not valid. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This could be shown by, for       |
|                                   | example                           |

|                                   |     claims for the Pandemic Leave |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment and/or       |
|                                   |     different emergency payments, |
|                                   |     including the Australian      |
|                                   |     Government Disaster Recovery  |
|                                   |     Payment (AGDRP), New Zealand  |

|                                   |     DRP), Disaster Recovery       |
|                                   |     Allowance (DRA) and New       |
|                                   |     Zealand Disaster Recovery     |
|                                   |     Allowance (NZ DRA)            |

|                                   |     concerns about fraud          |
|                                   | -   debt ACT DOCS completed on    |
|                                   |     record                        |
|                                   |     - Note: this is not a         |
|                                   |     complete list. Staff need to  |
|                                   |     consider details on the       |
|                                   |     customer’s record to          |
|                                   |     determine next steps.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are concerns, go to Step |
|                                   | 14                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A claim can be rejected with no   |
|                                   | further customer contact if:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a customer lodged a fifth or      |
|                                   | subsequent claim, and             |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | evidence to support that claim,   |
|                                   | and                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they withdrew that fifth or       |
|                                   | subsequent claim or that claim    |

|                                   | ‘Failed to Provide Information’   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they then lodged a new fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim without the      |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To reject the claim using the |

|                                   |     conditions of payment, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 34                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Continue to assess the claim if   |
|                                   | the customer has:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a fifth or subsequent  |
|                                   |     claim after a previous        |
|                                   |     withdrawal, and               |
|                                   | -   has provided all evidence     |
|                                   |     previously requested to       |
|                                   |     support previous claims paid  |
|                                   |     and their current claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if Real Time Analysis have  |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, if the customer does not |
|                                   |     meet the eligibility          |
|                                   |     criteria, the claim should be |

| 4                                 | Review Keywords and DOCs/Notes    |
|                                   | with specific titles + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Keywords may be added to a claim  |
|                                   | to indicate:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Some Pandemic Leave Disaster      |
|                                   | Payment claims are excluded from  |
|                                   | automation (straight through      |
|                                   | processing), where they do not    |
|                                   | meet the strict business rules to |
|                                   | enable the system to determine a  |
|                                   | grant outcome and need a manual   |
|                                   | assessment to be completed to     |
|                                   | make sure the accuracy of the     |
|                                   | outcome The most common exclusion |
|                                   | reasons will show on the Keywords |
|                                   | page to help staff in processing  |
|                                   | claims. See Resources for the     |
|                                   | list of hold reasons and keywords |
|                                   | Note: when a claim is excluded    |
|                                   | from automation, the customer may |
|                                   | still be eligible for payment.    |
|                                   | While an exclusion reason may     |
|                                   | show, this is not the only reason |
|                                   | the claim may have been excluded  |
|                                   | from automation. Service Officers |
|                                   | must review the claim fully,      |
|                                   | including the exclusion reason,   |
|                                   | when determining if a customer is |
|                                   | eligible or ineligible for the    |
|                                   | payment                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Action needed for the claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Resources for a list of   |
|                                   |     hold reasons and keywords     |
|                                   |     used in Process Direct        |
|                                   | -   Select the Keywords icon      |
|                                   | -   Depending on the keyword/s    |
|                                   |     listed and information in     |
|                                   |     Notes or DOCs as per the      |
|                                   |     Review Notes/DOCs step        |
|                                   |     continue to assess the claim  |
|                                   |     if appropriate, go to Step 5  |
|                                   |     - if Notes or DOCs indicate a |
|                                   |     claim can be granted or       |
|                                   |     rejected with no further      |
|                                   |     assessment, go to Step 34     |
|                                   |     - if Notes or DOCs indicate a |
|                                   |     claim has come off hold due   |
|                                   |     to a fifth or subsequent      |
|                                   |     claim, go to Table 7 > Step 9 |
|                                   |     - if Notes or DOCs indicate a |
|                                   |     claim lodged online has come  |
|                                   |     off hold as a customer was    |
|                                   |     asked to provide evidence     |
|                                   |     within 7 days to support a    |
|                                   |     late claim lodged, go to      |
|                                   |     Table 3 Step 6. Note:         |
|                                   |     customers should not be able  |
|                                   |     to lodge a late claim online. |
|                                   |     Staff who put the claim on    |
|                                   |     hold should have raised an    |
|                                   |     incident via Roxy. If not,    |
|                                   |     raise the incident            |
|                                   |     - If there is a ‘To be read   |
|                                   |     for PLDP claim’ DOC/Note, a   |
|                                   |     customer was advised during   |
|                                   |     an Assisted Customer Claim    |
|                                   |     (ACC) to provide evidence     |
|                                   |     within 7 days to support      |
|                                   |     their claim (this may have    |
|                                   |     been due to a previously      |
|                                   |     withdrawn claim/s or where    |
|                                   |     staff had concerns about the  |
|                                   |     validity of the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim). The ‘Channel’ of the  |
|                                   |     claim will show as INTERNAL.  |
|                                   |     Check for any evidence        |
|                                   |     uploaded and any details in   |
|                                   |     the Progress of claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section.   |
|                                   |     If the requested evidence has |
|                                   |     not been uploaded, reject the |
|                                   |     claim with no further         |
|                                   |     customer contact. Go to Step  |
|                                   |     34                            |
|                                   |     - If there is a ‘PLDP late    |
|                                   |     claim accepted’ DOC/Note, a   |
|                                   |     customer was advised during   |
|                                   |     an ACC they meet special      |
|                                   |     reasons for a late claim. The |
|                                   |     ‘Channel’ of the claim will   |
|                                   |     show as INTERNAL See Table 4  |
|                                   |     in Pandemic Leave Disaster    |
|                                   |     Payment - Assisted Customer   |
|                                   |     Claims                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim is under review by a        |
|                                   | specialist fraud team. If the     |
|                                   | keyword:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   FRDCHK is listed, do not      |
|                                   |     action the claim              |
|                                   |     - In Main Category select WLM |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi-Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign the claim with       |
|                                   |     Reason of Recategorised       |
|                                   |     - Note: if the option         |
|                                   |     Recategorised does not work,  |
|                                   |     select User unavailable       |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   |     -The claim will then be       |
|                                   |     allocated to an appropriately |
|                                   |     trained Service Officer to    |
|                                   |     make the assessment           |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim has been reviewed by a      |
|                                   | specialist fraud team and is      |
|                                   | cleared to be processed. If the   |
|                                   | keyword:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   FRDASS is listed, the claim   |
|                                   |     has been cleared of integrity |
|                                   |     risks and qualification       |
|                                   |     should be assessed as normal  |
|                                   | -   FRDREJ is listed, reject the  |
|                                   |     claim. Note: no customer      |
|                                   |     contact is needed before      |
|                                   |     rejecting the claim           |
|                                   | -   If the keywords FRDCHK or     |
|                                   |     FRDREJ are not listed, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |

| 5                                 | Claim status + Read more ...      |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the claim status In Process?   |

|                                   | and functions                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Hold reasons: consider        |

|                                   |     evidence/POI has been         |

| 6                                 | Has a decision already been made  |
|                                   | on the customer's claim for the   |
|                                   | exact same claim period? + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A new claim decision cannot be    |
|                                   | made when a customer is trying to |
|                                   | claim for the exact same claim    |
|                                   | period.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer has been paid |
|                                   | for an overlapping period this is |
|                                   | checked later. If a customer has  |
|                                   | been rejected for an overlapping  |
|                                   | period, this should be considered |
|                                   | a new claim and assessed          |
|                                   | accordingly.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a decision has already been    |
|                                   | made for the exact same claim     |
|                                   | period, the customer would have   |
|                                   | received a decision letter. This  |
|                                   | tells them they can request an    |
|                                   | explanation (review) of the       |
|                                   | decision. New information can be  |
|                                   | discussed as part of that process |
|                                   | and a new decision made.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To check if a decision has been   |
|                                   | made on the customer's claim for  |
|                                   | the exact same claim period, key  |
|                                   | ‘DL’ in the Super Key field.      |
|                                   | Check the claim period in any     |
|                                   | relevant:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Finalisation notes            |
|                                   | -   Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment Grant Fast Note       |
|                                   | -   Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment Reject Fast Note      |
|                                   | -   DEP DOCs                      |
|                                   | -   CSO CLM EXG PLDP review ACC   |
|                                   |     run DOC                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is a CSO CLM EXG PLDP    |
|                                   | review ACC run DOC that includes  |
|                                   | the exact same claim period, the  |
|                                   | claim must be granted because of  |
|                                   | a completed explanation (review)  |
|                                   | of a decision. Select Next to     |
|                                   | progress through the claim to the |
|                                   | Claim Decision screen. Go to Step |
|                                   | 25.                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has a decision been made for the  |
|                                   | exact same claim period and there |
|                                   | is no CSO CLM EXG PLDP review ACC |
|                                   | run DOC on record for the same    |
|                                   | period?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Status icon        |
|                                   |     [Status] from the menu bar    |
|                                   | -   Select the Edit icon [] to    |
|                                   |     change the status             |
|                                   | -   The Change Status screen will |
|                                   |     show. Select Not effective    |
|                                   |     from the Status drop down     |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Notes icon [Notes]     |
|                                   |     from the menu bar             |
|                                   | -   Select the Add Document icon  |
|                                   |     []                            |
|                                   | -   Category: select Claim from   |
|                                   |     the drop down                 |
|                                   | -   Summary: Type in this field   |
|                                   |     PLDP claim                    |
|                                   | -   Content: clearly document:    |
|                                   |     - claim ID                    |
|                                   |     - state or territory claimed  |
|                                   |     - self isolation, quarantine  |
|                                   |     or caring period claimed      |
|                                   |     - that a claim decision has   |
|                                   |     already been made             |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer record. This     |
|                                   |     will go back to the Process   |
|                                   |     Direct Landing Page. To be    |
|                                   |     allocated another claim to    |
|                                   |     assess, select the Inbox      |
|                                   |     icon, then select Ready       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 7                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Transaction Summary screen + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The claim will open in the        |
|                                   | Transaction Summary (TS) screen.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if the Error Message SR439  |
|                                   | Customer in Environment I shows,  |
|                                   | the record is in Environment I. A |
|                                   | claim processed in this           |
|                                   | environment will not finalise.    |
|                                   | The customer’s record must be     |
|                                   | transferred to the local          |
|                                   | environment in Customer First     |
|                                   | before continuing. See ICOA       |
|                                   | Transfer of a Customer Record     |
|                                   | using Customer First or Customer  |
|                                   | Record. For help, contact         |
|                                   | Technical Peer Support. When the  |
|                                   | environment transfer is complete, |
|                                   | continue the claim process in     |
|                                   | Process Direct.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the ‘Channel’ of the claim. |
|                                   | If it shows as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | WEB CHANNEL, this is an online    |
|                                   | claim lodged by a customer and    |
|                                   | the customer will meet the        |
|                                   | identity requirements             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘Submitted by’ will show the  |
|                                   |     customer’s CRN                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | INTERNAL this is a phone claim    |
|                                   | lodged using Assisted Customer    |
|                                   | Claim (ACC).                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | WEB CHANNEL go to Step 8          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | INTERNAL - if the identity status |
|                                   | shows:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirmed, go to Step 8           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not Confirmed, select the         |
|                                   | Identity not confirmed link to go |
|                                   | to the identity confirmation      |
|                                   | dashboard. If the Identity        |
|                                   | Confirmation Dashboard does not   |
|                                   | open, key START next to Super     |
|                                   | Key, tick Identity confirmation,  |
|                                   | and select the green Start button |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Next to continue and   |
|                                   |     go to Step 8 if an            |
|                                   |     Alternative identity, or one  |
|                                   |     identity document from each   |
|                                   |     of the following categories,  |
|                                   |     has been coded:               |
|                                   |     - Commencement of Identity    |
|                                   |     (CoI) Document                |
|                                   |     - Primary Use in Community    |
|                                   |     (PUiC) Document               |
|                                   |     - Secondary Use in Community  |
|                                   |     (SUiC) Document               |
|                                   | -   If these documents do not     |
|                                   |     show as verified, from the    |
|                                   |     menu bar (this may be because |
|                                   |     identity requirements were    |
|                                   |     not checked and completed     |
|                                   |     during the customer’s phone   |
|                                   |     claim), select Documents.     |
|                                   |     Check if any identity         |
|                                   |     documents have been uploaded  |
|                                   |     by the customer. If they      |
|                                   |     have, and the customer meets  |
|                                   |     all other eligibility         |
|                                   |     criteria, the customer should |
|                                   |     be contacted after assessing  |
|                                   |     all other claim details, as   |
|                                   |     they will need to provide     |
|                                   |     consent for these to be coded |
|                                   |     in the Identity Confirmation  |
|                                   |     Dashboard                     |
|                                   | -   Reject the claim if an        |
|                                   |     Alternative identity, or one  |
|                                   |     identity document from each   |
|                                   |     of the categories above, has  |
|                                   |     not been coded                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | View Claim Summary + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Open the Claim Summary by     |
|                                   |     selecting [Open left slider;  |
|                                   |     Close right slider]at the top |
|                                   |     left of the screen, just      |
|                                   |     above the Super Key           |
|                                   | -   The Claim Summary shows the   |
|                                   |     answers the customer provided |
|                                   |     to the claim questions.       |
|                                   | -   Staff can select Enter Full   |
|                                   |     Screen [Enter full screen] to |
|                                   |     expand the claim overview to  |
|                                   |     full screen in a separate     |
|                                   |     window and move this to a     |
|                                   |     second screen (if possible)   |
|                                   | -   Refer to the Claim Summary    |
|                                   |     while assessing and coding    |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   | -   Note: customers self-declare  |
|                                   |     all information in their      |
|                                   |     claim. The following steps    |
|                                   |     are checks staff must         |
|                                   |     complete before finalising a  |
|                                   |     claim outcome                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims lodged on or after 27  |
|                                   | April 2022                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers can make a              |
|                                   | self-declaration that they meet   |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Australian Government     |
|                                   |     definition of close contact,  |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   the close contact definition  |
|                                   |     in their state or territory   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff do not need to:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   check which definition is     |
|                                   |     met, or                       |
|                                   | -   refer to state or territory   |
|                                   |     close contact definitions, or |
|                                   | -   find out if a customer meets  |
|                                   |     a state or territory close    |
|                                   |     contact definition            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For claims lodged on or after 8   |
|                                   | May 2022                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The online claim has been updated |
|                                   | to direct customers to check      |
|                                   | their state or territory          |
|                                   | government requirements regarding |
|                                   | self-isolation and quarantine     |
|                                   | rules. This is due to recent      |
|                                   | changes some states and           |
|                                   | territories have made to close    |
|                                   | contact rules.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Options to select in the online   |
|                                   | claim around the need to          |
|                                   | self-isolate for close contact    |
|                                   | impact reasons have been updated  |
|                                   | to include                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a person’s state or territory |
|                                   |     government requires them to   |
|                                   |     isolate, or                   |
|                                   | -   a person’s employer has       |
|                                   |     directed them not to attend   |
|                                   |     their workplace even though   |
|                                   |     their state or territory      |
|                                   |     government does not require   |
|                                   |     them to self-isolate          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff do not need to:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | check state or territory          |
|                                   | government rules about the        |
|                                   | requirements to self-isolate or   |
|                                   | quarantine                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | find out if a customer should or  |
|                                   | should not self-isolate or        |
|                                   | quarantine                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   under their state or          |
|                                   |     territory government rules,   |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   due to being directed by      |
|                                   |     their employer not to attend  |
|                                   |     work                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Close contact.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim summary shows the    |
|                                   | customer has:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged their claim within 14  |
|                                   |     days from and including the   |
|                                   |     first day of their 7 day      |
|                                   |     claiming period (see the      |
|                                   |     ‘Start date of the 7 day      |
|                                   |     period’ in the Claim          |
|                                   |     Summary), go to Step 9        |
|                                   | -   a self-isolation, quarantine  |
|                                   |     or caring period that started |
|                                   |     between 1 July and 20 July    |
|                                   |     2022 (inclusive) and the      |
|                                   |     customer has lodged their     |
|                                   |     claim before 11:59 pm Eastern |
|                                   |     Standard Time on 2 August     |
|                                   |     2022, because of the          |
|                                   |     re-instatement of the payment |
|                                   |     in July 2022, go to Step 9    |
|                                   | -   not lodged their claim within |
|                                   |     14 days from and including    |
|                                   |     the first day of their 7 day  |
|                                   |     claiming period (see the      |
|                                   |     ‘Start date of the 7 day      |
|                                   |     period’ in the Claim          |
|                                   |     Summary), and at the          |
|                                   |     Transaction Summary step      |
|                                   |     (above) the claim channel     |
|                                   |     identified was ONLINE, this   |
|                                   |     is a system issue. Raise an   |
|                                   |     incident via Roxy quoting     |
|                                   |     'Claim lodged outside 14      |
|                                   |     days'. Note this information  |
|                                   |     for later and continue to     |
|                                   |     assess the claim. Note: if    |
|                                   |     all other eligibility         |
|                                   |     criteria are met, customer    |
|                                   |     contact will be needed to     |
|                                   |     decide if they have a special |
|                                   |     reason for their late claim.  |
|                                   |     Go to Step 9                  |
|                                   | -   the entire 7 day period in    |
|                                   |     ‘Period of time I’ll provide  |
|                                   |     care for this person’ occurs  |
|                                   |     before the ‘Start date of the |
|                                   |     7 day period,’ this is a      |
|                                   |     system issue. For example,    |
|                                   |     the ‘Period of time I’ll      |
|                                   |     provide care for this person’ |
|                                   |     states ‘care provided for     |
|                                   |     this person from 27 April to  |
|                                   |     3 May 2022’ and ‘Start date   |
|                                   |     of the 7 day period’ states   |
|                                   |     ‘I am claiming from 6 May     |
|                                   |     2022.’ For help, contact      |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support        |
|                                   |     - raise an incident via Roxy  |
|                                   |     quoting ' Entire period of    |
|                                   |     care occurs before the start  |
|                                   |     date of the 7 day claim       |
|                                   |     period'. Note this            |
|                                   |     information for later and     |
|                                   |     continue to assess the claim. |
|                                   |     Note: if all other            |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria are met, |
|                                   |     customer contact will be      |
|                                   |     needed                        |
|                                   |     - go to Step 9                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Check income support payment      |
|                                   | (ISP) – current, zero rate or     |
|                                   | cancelled, Parental Leave Pay     |
|                                   | (PPL) or Dad and Partner Pay      |
|                                   | (DAP) + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has voluntarily     |
|                                   | cancelled their JobSeeker Payment |
|                                   | (JSP) or Youth Allowance (YA) in  |
|                                   | the 28 days before the start date |
|                                   | of the 7 day period they are      |
|                                   | claiming the Pandemic leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment, further action  |
|                                   | is needed.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To make sure the customer has not |
|                                   | received an ISP (including a zero |
|                                   | rate), PPL or DAP on any day of   |
|                                   | the 7 day period claimed, check   |
|                                   | the:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Benefit Status line on the        |
|                                   | Customer Summary screen:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Receiving an ISP will show as |
|                                   |     CUR                           |
|                                   | -   Zero rate will show as CZR    |
|                                   |     ('zero rate' does not include |
|                                   |     customers with a pending,     |
|                                   |     assessed (ASS) or suspended   |
|                                   |     (SUS) status)                 |
|                                   | -   Received DAP will show as     |
|                                   |     DAP/PAY                       |
|                                   | -   Claiming for DAP will show as |
|                                   |     DAP/NCL, DAP/PND or DAP/ASS   |
|                                   | -   Receiving PPL will show as    |
|                                   |     PPL/CUR                       |
|                                   | -   Awaiting a flexible PPL day   |
|                                   |     will show as PPL/CZR-FLX      |
|                                   | -   Claiming for PPL will show as |
|                                   |     PPL/NCL or PPL/ASS            |
|                                   | -   Cancelled JSP or YA will show |
|                                   |     as JSP/CAN-CLR or YAL/CAN-CLR |
|                                   |     - To check if the customer    |
|                                   |     has voluntarily cancelled JSP |
|                                   |     or YA in the 28 days before   |
|                                   |     the start date of the 7 day   |
|                                   |     period they are claiming the  |
|                                   |     Pandemic leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment, key ABH in the Super |
|                                   |     Key to go to the Payment      |
|                                   |     History Summary.              |
|                                   |     - If Type is JSP or YAL,      |
|                                   |     Status is CAN and Reason is   |
|                                   |     WITHDRAWN/VOLUNTARY           |
|                                   |     SURRENDER, this means the     |
|                                   |     customer has voluntarily      |
|                                   |     cancelled their JSP or YA.    |
|                                   |     Check the date under Date of  |
|                                   |     event to determine if they    |
|                                   |     have cancelled in the 28 days |
|                                   |     before the start date of the  |
|                                   |     7 day period they are         |
|                                   |     claiming the Pandemic leave   |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment.             |
|                                   |     - These claims may have the   |
|                                   |     keyword STP360 listed         |
|                                   |     - If the customer has done    |
|                                   |     this, go to Step 12           |
|                                   |     - Otherwise, keep assessing   |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   | -   Has a status of SUS/IMP or    |
|                                   |     CAN/IMP and meets all         |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 11                       |
|                                   | -   Youth Bonus Wage Subsidy      |
|                                   |     customers will show as        |
|                                   |     JSP/SUS-YBS or YAL/SUS-YBS.   |
|                                   |     These customers are not       |
|                                   |     receiving an ISP              |
|                                   | -   Receiving the Home Equity     |
|                                   |     Access Scheme will show as    |
|                                   |     (primary benefit)/(status),   |
|                                   |     for example, AGE/CZR – PLS.   |
|                                   |     Continue assessing the        |
|                                   |     customer’s claim. If the      |
|                                   |     customer meets all other      |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria, these   |
|                                   |     claims will need to be        |
|                                   |     escalated to Technical Peer   |
|                                   |     Support and a payment query   |
|                                   |     template completed. Do not do |
|                                   |     this yet. Continue assessing  |
|                                   |     the claim to make sure all    |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria    |
|                                   |     are met                       |
|                                   | -   ABSTUDY customers will show   |
|                                   |     as ABY/CUR. If ABY/CUR shows: |
|                                   |     - go to the Education Details |
|                                   |     (EDC) screen to find the      |
|                                   |     current course of study       |
|                                   |     recorded                      |
|                                   |     - if the participation status |
|                                   |     is FTI, API or PTS, the       |
|                                   |     customer meets the            |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria          |
|                                   |     - if any other code shows,    |
|                                   |     the customer does not meet    |
|                                   |     the eligibility criteria.     |
|                                   |     Keep selecting Next to        |
|                                   |     continue. At the Claim        |
|                                   |     Decision screen, go to Step   |
|                                   |     34                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Department of Veterans’ Affairs   |
|                                   | (DVA) screen to see if the        |
|                                   | customer is receiving a Service   |
|                                   | Pension or Veteran payment        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Allowance Benefit History (ABH)   |
|                                   | screen to see when the customer   |
|                                   | started receiving their ISP:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type: shows the code of the   |
|                                   |     payment the customer was      |
|                                   |     receiving (for example JSP or |
|                                   |     DSP)                          |
|                                   | -   Status: must be CUR or CZR    |
|                                   | -   DOE (date of effect): shows   |
|                                   |     the date the customer became  |
|                                   |     eligible for the payment, and |
|                                   | -   Pensions Status History       |
|                                   |     (PNSH) screen to see when the |
|                                   |     customer started receiving a  |
|                                   |     pension payment:              |
|                                   | -   Type: shows the code of the   |
|                                   |     payment the customer was      |
|                                   |     receiving (for example AGE or |
|                                   |     DSP)                          |
|                                   | -   Status: must be CUR or CZR    |
|                                   | -   DOE (date of effect): shows   |
|                                   |     the date the customer became  |
|                                   |     eligible for the payment      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Benefit Status (XBS) screen to    |
|                                   | see when the customer started     |
|                                   | receiving various payment types   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Change the System to:         |
|                                   |     - ALL - to see a list of      |
|                                   |     multiple payment types        |
|                                   |     - PEN - AGE, DSP, CAR, PPS    |
|                                   |     - NSS - JSP, YA, WA, SpB, AUS |
|                                   |     - PGA - PPP                   |
|                                   |     - ISS DAP, PPL, FHA, ABY,     |
|                                   |     FSP - including DRA, CDP. If  |
|                                   |     receiving DRA, see Customers  |
|                                   |     claiming the Pandemic Leave   |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment and DRA or   |
|                                   |     NZ DRA and Scenarios          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Payment Summary (PS) screen to    |
|                                   | confirm the customer has been     |
|                                   | receiving an ISP during the 7 day |
|                                   | claim period:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   In ‘Display payments for’     |
|                                   |     change to ‘all’               |
|                                   | -   In ‘Number of months in past’ |
|                                   |     change to 12                  |
|                                   | -   Select payments before,       |
|                                   |     during and after the period   |
|                                   |     the customer is applying for  |
|                                   |     to determine the period the   |
|                                   |     payments apply to             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If DAP/PAY, DAP Period Rate       |
|                                   | Explanation (REXDAP). Note: this  |
|                                   | screen does not exist in Process  |
|                                   | Direct, this will have to be      |
|                                   | checked in Customer First.        |
|                                   | (Staff should not have the        |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors. Select the Home     |
|                                   | button at the top left hand side  |
|                                   | to exit out of the transaction    |
|                                   | and the customer’s record. This   |
|                                   | will go back to the Process       |
|                                   | Direct Landing Page. Go to        |
|                                   | Customer First to check this      |
|                                   | information. Once the customer’s  |
|                                   | record is closed in Customer      |
|                                   | First, return to the customer’s   |
|                                   | claim in Process Direct)          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This will show the customer’s |
|                                   |     full DAP period               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If DAP/NCL, DAP/PND or DAP/ASS:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Transactions            |
|                                   | -   Select the customer’s DAP     |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   Select [Open left slider;     |
|                                   |     Close right slider] to review |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   | -   The DAP period start date is  |
|                                   |     the date the customer         |
|                                   |     nominates to start their DAP  |
|                                   |     payment from.                 |
|                                   | -   The DAP period end date is    |
|                                   |     any of the following that     |
|                                   |     occurs first for the          |
|                                   |     customer:                     |
|                                   |     - worked or received paid     |
|                                   |     leave                         |
|                                   |     - stopped caring for the      |
|                                   |     child, or                     |
|                                   |     - 14 days after the start     |
|                                   |     date                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If PPL/NCL:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to Search Online Claims    |
|                                   | -   select the customer's PPL     |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   refer to the Additional child |
|                                   |     details section for the PPL   |
|                                   |     start date and the Flexible   |
|                                   |     PPL Options for the Flexible  |
|                                   |     PPL claim information         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If PPL/CUR, PPL/CAN, PPL/ASS or   |
|                                   | PPL/CZR-FLX:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   key ‘P1RCS’ in the Super Key  |
|                                   |     field to go to the PPL        |
|                                   |     Calculation Summary (P1RCS)   |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   select the > (Expand for      |
|                                   |     details) icon to view the PPL |
|                                   |     claim details, including the  |
|                                   |     PPL period and the connected  |
|                                   |     days                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | is not receiving an ISP, PPL or   |
|                                   | DAP on any day of the 7 day       |
|                                   | period they are claiming the      |
|                                   | customer is eligible to receive   |
|                                   | the Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment if they meet all other    |
|                                   | eligibility criteria              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Next to continue       |
|                                   | -   go to Step 12                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | is receiving an ISP (including a  |
|                                   | zero rate), DAP or PPL (except    |
|                                   | PPL/CZR-FLX) on any day of the 7  |
|                                   | day period they are claiming      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The customer does not meet    |
|                                   |     the eligibility criteria      |
|                                   | -   No further customer contact   |
|                                   |     is needed                     |
|                                   | -   Keep selecting Next to        |
|                                   |     continue                      |
|                                   | -   At the Claim Decision screen, |
|                                   |     go to Step 34                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | has a:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   pending, new claim (NCL),     |
|                                   |     assessed (ASS) or suspended   |
|                                   |     (SUS) status (except for      |
|                                   |     JSP/SUS-YBS or YAL/SUS-YBS)   |
|                                   | -   DAP/NCL, DAP/PND or DAP/ASS   |
|                                   |     where the period overlaps     |
|                                   |     with the Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment period, or   |
|                                   | -   PPL/NCL, PPL/CZR-FLX or       |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Customer has a pending, assessed  |
|                                   | (ASS) or suspended (SUS) ISP, or  |
|                                   | overlapping DAP/NCL, DAP/PND,     |
|                                   | DAP/ASS, PPL/NCL, PPL/CZR-FLX or  |
|                                   | PPL/ASS period + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers with a pending, ASS or  |
|                                   | SUS ISP due to their ISP status,  |
|                                   | a staff member who is trained in  |
|                                   | the relevant ISP may need to      |
|                                   | speak with the customer.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers with a status of        |
|                                   | DAP/NCL, DAP/PND, DAP/ASS,        |
|                                   | PPL/NCL, PPL/CZR-FLX or PPL/ASS   |
|                                   | also should speak with a staff    |
|                                   | member trained in the relevant    |
|                                   | payment if their DAP or PPL may   |
|                                   | overlap with their Pandemic Leave |
|                                   | Disaster Payment claim period.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Pending ISP                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check DOCs for a Pending ISP      |
|                                   | Progress of Claim DOC or Note by  |
|                                   | keying ‘DL’ in the Super Key      |
|                                   | field.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NCL, ASS and SUS ISP              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the Benefit Status line on  |
|                                   | the Transaction Summary (TS)      |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   An 'Assessed' ISP will show   |
|                                   |     as ASS                        |
|                                   | -   A 'Suspended' ISP will show   |
|                                   |     as SUS                        |
|                                   | -   A ‘New claim’ pending         |
|                                   |     assessment will show as NCL   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer meet all other  |
|                                   | eligibility criteria and have a   |
|                                   | pending, assessed or suspended    |
|                                   | ISP, or status of DAP/NCL,        |
|                                   | DAP/PND, DAP/ASS, PPL/NCL,        |
|                                   | PPL/CZR-FLX or PPL/ASS?           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For staff trained in the      |
|                                   |     relevant ISP, DAP or PPL,     |
|                                   |     assess the customer's         |
|                                   |     individual circumstances      |
|                                   | -   Some DAP or PPL customers may |
|                                   |     need to move their DAP period |
|                                   |     start date, PPL period start  |
|                                   |     date or Flexible PPL days to  |
|                                   |     prevent the payment           |
|                                   |     overlapping the Pandemic      |
|                                   |     Leave Disaster Payment        |
|                                   | -   If the customer meets all     |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria    |
|                                   |     and their record shows they   |
|                                   |     could receive an ISP on any   |
|                                   |     day of the 7 day period they  |
|                                   |     are claiming, contact the     |
|                                   |     customer to discuss their     |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   | -   If the customer:              |
|                                   |     - can proceed with their      |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claim, noting that    |
|                                   |     customers with a suspended    |
|                                   |     ISP must cancel this to       |
|                                   |     receive a Pandemic Leave      |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment, select Next |
|                                   |     to continue. Go to Step 13    |
|                                   |     - does not wish to or cannot  |
|                                   |     proceed with their Pandemic   |
|                                   |     Leave Disaster Payment claim, |
|                                   |     the customer will need to     |
|                                   |     withdraw their claim          |
|                                   | -   For staff not trained in the  |
|                                   |     relevant ISP, DAP or PPL,     |
|                                   |     continue assessing the claim  |
|                                   |     - if the customer meets all   |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria,   |
|                                   |     continue assessing the claim. |
|                                   |     A later step advises to add a |
|                                   |     keyword to the claim, for the |
|                                   |     claim to be allocated to a    |
|                                   |     staff member trained in the   |
|                                   |     relevant ISP, DAP or PPL.     |
|                                   |     However, do not do this yet   |
|                                   |     - select Next to continue     |
|                                   |     - go to Step 13               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 13                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 11                                | Customer has an ISP status of     |
|                                   | SUS/IMP or CAN/IMP + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer did not have an ISP |
|                                   | status of SUS/IMP or CAN/IMP      |
|                                   | (this would have been identified  |
|                                   | at the Check ISP step above), go  |
|                                   | to Step 12.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers with an ISP status of   |
|                                   | SUS/IMP or CAN/IMP may be in      |
|                                   | gaol.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customers cannot receive the      |
|                                   | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | if they are in gaol.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key ‘DL’ in the Super Key field   |
|                                   | to go to the customer’s Document  |
|                                   | List (DL) screen to check for a   |
|                                   | DOC that confirms the customer    |
|                                   | has been released from gaol.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no DOC, more details  |
|                                   | are needed from the customer to   |
|                                   | progress their claim, see Table   |
|                                   | 3.                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer details needed:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the name of the facility they |
|                                   |     were released from,           |
|                                   | -   the date they were released   |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   | -   their MIN (Master Index       |
|                                   |     Number), this is their prison |
|                                   |     reference number              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the customer in gaol?          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, reject the claim         |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 13             |
