| 12                                | Customer voluntarily cancelled    |
|                                   | JSP or YA in the 28 days before   |
|                                   | the start date of the 7 day       |
|                                   | period claimed + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |
|                                   | in the Check income support       |
|                                   | payment (ISP) step                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has not           |
|                                   | voluntarily cancelled JSP or YA   |
|                                   | in the 28 days before the start   |
|                                   | date of the 7 day period they are |
|                                   | claiming the Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment, go to Step 13   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If they have voluntarily          |
|                                   | cancelled JSP or YA in the 28     |
|                                   | days before the start date of the |
|                                   | 7 day period they are claiming    |
|                                   | the Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment, check income recorded as |
|                                   | part of their last payment        |
|                                   | period.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Screens in Process Direct may     |
|                                   | display different information and |
|                                   | cannot be used for this step      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page.      |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key PS in the Next field, then    |
|                                   | press [Enter] to go to the        |
|                                   | Payment Summary (PS) screen       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Next to Display payments for:     |
|                                   | select NSS from the drop down     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the last date recorded in   |
|                                   | the Paid to column, including a   |
|                                   | zero rate                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select this payment by clicking   |
|                                   | on the link in the Delivery Date  |
|                                   | column                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Payment Details (PD) screen   |
|                                   | will then open                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note down the dates next to Rgp:  |
|                                   | or Stm:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key NIS in the Next field, then   |
|                                   | press [Enter] to go to the NSS    |
|                                   | Income Summary (NIS) screen       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note down the date next to Date   |
|                                   | From:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Only consider income under the    |
|                                   | Customer column (not the Partner  |
|                                   | column) and payment amounts next  |
|                                   | to the following fields           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Gross EMp Inc (cas):          |
|                                   | -   Gross EMp Inc (cont):         |
|                                   | -   Real Est/Bus (E)              |
|                                   | -   Real Est/Bus (U)              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the NIS screen shows income    |
|                                   | next to Real Est/Bus (E) or Real  |
|                                   | Est/Bus (U)                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key REBS in the Next field,   |
|                                   |     then press [Enter] to go to   |
|                                   |     the Real Estate/Business      |
|                                   |     Summary (REBS) screen         |
|                                   | -   Check that income is from     |
|                                   |     self-employment only          |
|                                   | -   If any real estate or trust   |
|                                   |     income shows do not consider  |
|                                   |     this                          |
|                                   | -   For help, contact Technical   |
|                                   |     Peer Support                  |
|                                   | -   Note down if it is clear      |
|                                   |     there is income from          |
|                                   |     self-employment               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer has met the Pandemic |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment            |
|                                   | requirement of declaring income   |
|                                   | in the payment period before      |
|                                   | cancelling JSP or YA when all the |
|                                   | following apply                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the date next to Date From: falls |
|                                   | in between the dates noted next   |
|                                   | to Rgp: or Stm: in the PD screen, |
|                                   | and                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | there are payment amounts next to |
|                                   | the following fields in the NIS   |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Gross EMp Inc (cas):          |
|                                   | -   Gross EMp Inc (cont):         |
|                                   | -   Real Est/Bus (E)              |
|                                   | -   Real Est/Bus (U), and         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | if there is income in the REBS    |
|                                   | screen next to Real Est/Bus (E)   |
|                                   | or Real Est/Bus (U), it is clear  |
|                                   | this is income from               |
|                                   | self-employment                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer met the Pandemic |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment            |
|                                   | requirement of declaring income   |
|                                   | in the payment period before      |
|                                   | cancelling JSP or YA?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, the customer has reported    |
|                                   | employment or self-employment     |
|                                   | income in their last payment      |
|                                   | period, and has shown they had    |
|                                   | employment or self-employment     |
|                                   | income immediately before         |
|                                   | claiming the Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Close the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   | -   Return to the customer’s      |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 13                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, the customer has not reported |
|                                   | employment or self-employment     |
|                                   | income in their last payment      |
|                                   | period, and has not shown they    |
|                                   | had employment or self-employment |
|                                   | income immediately before         |
|                                   | claiming the Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer meets all     |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria:   |
|                                   |     - Note this information for   |
|                                   |     later                         |
|                                   |     - Do not reject the claim     |
|                                   |     - Follow up will be needed    |
|                                   |     later to request evidence     |
|                                   |     from the customer. Note:      |
|                                   |     follow all relevant steps in  |
|                                   |     this table. A later step will |
|                                   |     advise when to see Table 9    |
|                                   |     - Close the customer’s record |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   |     - Return to the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   |     - Go to Step 13               |

| 13                                | Customer is caring for a child 16 |
|                                   | years or under in their care or a |
|                                   | person with a disability or       |
|                                   | severe medical condition + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer is not claiming     |
|                                   | under a caring impact reason, go  |
|                                   | to Step 14                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Due to system limitations, staff  |
|                                   | only need to check this if a      |
|                                   | customer has a partner.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Relations [] menu       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer does not have a   |
|                                   | partner + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 14                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has a partner +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If caring due to a :              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | close contact impact reason -     |
|                                   | there can only be one claim made  |
|                                   | due to caring for that child or   |
|                                   | person with a disability or       |
|                                   | severe medical condition, even if |
|                                   | the self-isolation, quarantine or |
|                                   | caring period is greater than 7   |
|                                   | days. That is, only one person    |
|                                   | can be paid due to caring for     |
|                                   | that child or person for the same |
|                                   | continuous or an overlapping      |
|                                   | self-isolation and caring period. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | positive COVID-19 test impact     |
|                                   | reason - there can be more than   |
|                                   | one claim made due to caring for  |
|                                   | that child or person with a       |
|                                   | severe medical condition or       |
|                                   | disability, if all of the         |
|                                   | following are met:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The self-isolation,           |
|                                   |     quarantine or caring period   |
|                                   |     is greater than 7 days, and   |
|                                   | -   A further claim for an        |
|                                   |     additional period is lodged   |
|                                   |     as the person being cared for |
|                                   |     still needs to isolate in the |
|                                   |     current period claimed        |
|                                   |     because of the effects of     |
|                                   |     COVID-19, and                 |
|                                   | -   Based on the period of        |
|                                   |     isolation and care being      |
|                                   |     different to the other        |
|                                   |     parent, the extension         |
|                                   |     questions have been asked in  |
|                                   |     the claim and answered in a   |
|                                   |     way that establishes          |
|                                   |     eligibility, and              |
|                                   | -   There are no overlapping      |
|                                   |     periods (even one day) with   |
|                                   |     any claims granted to the     |
|                                   |     other parent                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Eligibility for a second      |
|                                   | payment after the end of the      |
|                                   | first 7 day period.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer’s record. Check   |
|                                   | the Claim Summary                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note down the:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Period of time the customer   |
|                                   |     will provide care for the     |
|                                   |     person                        |
|                                   | -   Start date of the 7 day claim |
|                                   |     period                        |
|                                   | -   Name of the child or person   |
|                                   |     with a disability or severe   |
|                                   |     medical condition the         |
|                                   |     customer is claiming the      |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment                       |
|                                   | -   Person who tested positive    |
|                                   |     that caused the close contact |
|                                   |     status (if claiming under a   |
|                                   |     close contact impact reason)  |
|                                   | -   Date tested positive with     |
|                                   |     COVID-19 (if claiming under a |
|                                   |     tested positive with COVID-19 |
|                                   |     impact reason)                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Relations [] menu,       |
|                                   | select the partner’s record       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To check if the partner has       |
|                                   | claimed a payment for the same    |
|                                   | person being cared for:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type PLDP_PS in the Super Key |
|                                   |     field to go to the partner’s  |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment Summary (PLDP_PS)     |
|                                   |     screen to check if any        |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claims have been      |
|                                   |     ‘Completed’ and paid for any  |
|                                   |     periods that overlap with any |
|                                   |     period in the customer’s      |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   Note down any claim IDs       |
|                                   | -   Select the Transactions icon  |
|                                   |     [Transactions (if accessed    |
|                                   |     via Customer First Tile)] to  |
|                                   |     check if the partner has any  |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claims ‘In process’   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are no claims            |
|                                   | ‘Completed’ and paid or ‘In       |
|                                   | process’, go to Step 14           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are claims ‘Completed’   |
|                                   | and paid or ‘In process’, compare |
|                                   | the partner’s claim information   |
|                                   | in the Claim Summary with the     |
|                                   | information noted down (above)    |
|                                   | from the Claim Summary of the     |
|                                   | customer’s claim being assessed.  |
|                                   | Note: if there is a claim ‘In     |
|                                   | process’ that overlaps the        |
|                                   | customer’s claim for the same     |
|                                   | impact reason, a decision on both |
|                                   | claims is needed to determine who |
|                                   | is eligible. The earliest claim   |
|                                   | lodged should be granted (if all  |
|                                   | eligibility criteria are met).    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If caring due to a close contact  |
|                                   | impact reason, if there are       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | no overlapping periods (even one  |
|                                   | day) with the customer’s claim    |
|                                   | being assessed, go to Step 14     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | any overlapping periods (even one |
|                                   | day) with the customer’s claim    |
|                                   | being assessed, the customer does |
|                                   | not meet the eligibility criteria |
|                                   | and their claim must be rejected  |
|                                   | if the following details are the  |
|                                   | same:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the name of the child or      |
|                                   |     person with a disability or   |
|                                   |     severe medical condition, and |
|                                   | -   the name of the person who    |
|                                   |     tested positive that resulted |
|                                   |     in the close contact status   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If caring as a child has tested   |
|                                   | positive, if the 7 day claim      |
|                                   | period, is                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | exactly the same, the customer    |
|                                   | does not meet the eligibility     |
|                                   | criteria. Reject the claim        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | not the same (overlapping periods |
|                                   | can be accepted in limited        |
|                                   | circumstances), and the extension |
|                                   | questions have:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   not been completed (that is,  |
|                                   |     the customer has recorded in  |
|                                   |     their Claim Summary ‘The      |
|                                   |     period I am claiming for is   |
|                                   |     not an extension of an        |
|                                   |     isolation period I previously |
|                                   |     claimed for’) the customer    |
|                                   |     does not meet the eligibility |
|                                   |     criteria and overlapping      |
|                                   |     periods cannot be accepted in |
|                                   |     this instance. Reject the     |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   | -   have been completed (that is, |
|                                   |     the customer has recorded in  |
|                                   |     their Claim Summary ‘The      |
|                                   |     period I am claiming for is   |
|                                   |     an extension of an isolation  |
|                                   |     period I previously claimed   |
|                                   |     for’) overlapping periods can |
|                                   |     be accepted in this instance. |
|                                   |     Go to Step 14                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 14                                | Concerns about validity + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When assessing a claim, staff may |
|                                   | have concerns about the validity  |
|                                   | of the claim information or other |
|                                   | details on the customer’s record. |
|                                   | There may be                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | warning signs that a claim may be |
|                                   | fraudulent. It may be an odd      |
|                                   | feeling or inconsistencies in     |
|                                   | what the customer claims.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the following may have      |
|                                   | already been considered at the    |
|                                   | Review record and Note/DOCs step  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the customer is      |
|                                   | showing behaviour that may        |
|                                   | suggest their claim is not valid. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This could be shown by, for       |
|                                   | example                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a history of withdrawing      |
|                                   |     claims for the Pandemic Leave |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment and/or       |
|                                   |     different emergency payments, |
|                                   |     including the Australian      |
|                                   |     Government Disaster Recovery  |
|                                   |     Payment (AGDRP), New Zealand  |
|                                   |     Disaster Recovery Payment (NZ |
|                                   |     DRP), Disaster Recovery       |
|                                   |     Allowance (DRA) and New       |
|                                   |     Zealand Disaster Recovery     |
|                                   |     Allowance (NZ DRA)            |
|                                   | -   a DOA DOC relating to         |
|                                   |     concerns about fraud          |
|                                   | -   debt ACT DOCS completed on    |
|                                   |     record                        |
|                                   |     - Note: this is not a         |
|                                   |     complete list. Staff need to  |
|                                   |     consider details on the       |
|                                   |     customer’s record to          |
|                                   |     determine next steps          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are concerns about       |
|                                   | employer details provided, use    |
|                                   | the ABN Lookup. Do not try to     |
|                                   | contact the employer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: later steps will advise the |
|                                   | process to follow if:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a customer has not met the        |
|                                   | requirement of declaring income   |
|                                   | in the payment period before      |
|                                   | cancelling JSP or YA (this would  |
|                                   | have been identified in the       |
|                                   | Customer voluntarily cancelled    |
|                                   | JSP or YA step), and              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | there are no other warning signs  |
|                                   | that a claim may be fraudulent    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not follow this step for   |
|                                   |     these claims                  |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 15                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | no concerns about the validity of |
|                                   | information, go to Step 15        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | concerns about the validity of    |
|                                   | information, before submitting a  |
|                                   | fraud report, first try to review |
|                                   | the claim information and clarify |
|                                   | any concerns with the customer.   |
|                                   | Note: do not use the term 'fraud’ |
|                                   | when speaking to a customer or    |
|                                   | updating their record. If         |
|                                   | appropriate:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   see Emergency payments -      |
|                                   |     preventing fraud and Table 3  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After clarifying any concerns and |
|                                   | reviewing evidence (if            |
|                                   | applicable):                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Service Officer is unsure  |
|                                   | whether to report a situation     |
|                                   | that they think may be suspected  |
|                                   | fraud, contact Technical Peer     |
|                                   | Support                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If fraud concerns have been       |
|                                   | resolved, but the evidence        |
|                                   | requested to validate discussions |
|                                   | has not been provided, and the    |
|                                   | timeframe to lodge evidence:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   has expired, the claim should |
|                                   |     be rejected. See Table 2      |
|                                   | -   has not expired, place the    |
|                                   |     claim On Hold for a further   |
|                                   |     28 days using hold reason     |
|                                   |     ‘Customer to Provide          |
|                                   |     information’. Procedure ends  |
|                                   |     here                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If fraud concerns have been       |
|                                   | resolved, continue processing the |
|                                   | claim, go to Step 15              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Service Officer believes   |
|                                   | the customer has acted            |
|                                   | fraudulently:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not grant the claim        |
|                                   | -   See Table 8                   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 15                                | Processing the claim + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Under Customer and Activity       |
|                                   | Information, check the Links      |
|                                   | Summary (LS) under Circumstance   |
|                                   | Data in the menu bar.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has a payment     |
|                                   | nominee, the NOM line on LS will  |
|                                   | have NOP coded in the ‘To’        |
|                                   | column. Continue assessing the    |
|                                   | claim, however note that the      |
|                                   | claim may need to be handed over  |
|                                   | to appropriately trained staff to |
|                                   | finalise in the !FFAP screen. See |
|                                   | Customers with nominee            |
|                                   | arrangements.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key ‘PAS’ next to Super Key   |
|                                   |     and press [Enter] to go to    |
|                                   |     the Payment Destination       |
|                                   |     Summary (PAS) screen          |
|                                   | -   Check for an FSP payment      |
|                                   | -   If there is no FSP payment,   |
|                                   |     the claim will need to be     |
|                                   |     finalised in the !FFAP        |
|                                   |     screen. Note this down. Later |
|                                   |     steps will advise the process |
|                                   |     to follow                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before selecting Process, make    |
|                                   | sure the claim has been           |
|                                   | ‘regenerated ‘(Locating work step |
|                                   | above). If not, staff must select |
|                                   | [more options] then Regenerate.   |
|                                   | Note: selecting Regenerate will   |
|                                   | automatically update the          |
|                                   | Immigration Data Link             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Process at the bottom      |
|                                   | right hand side of the screen.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must select Process to      |
|                                   | prevent unnecessary errors.       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 16                                | Task selectors + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Warning and Errors (SWE)      |
|                                   | screen will show.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Task Selector will show the   |
|                                   | screens in the claim workflow.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Any information updated by the    |
|                                   | customer will display a ‘flag’    |
|                                   | [Provisional Data Flag] and will  |
|                                   | be automatically selected (a tick |
|                                   | will show in the box).            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The following are mandatory Task  |
|                                   | Selectors and will always be      |
|                                   | automatically selected:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Residency                     |
|                                   | -   Payment Destination Details,  |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   | -   Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff can manually select other   |
|                                   | screens to view by ticking:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the corresponding box, or     |
|                                   | -   ‘Select all tasks’            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next at the bottom right   |
|                                   | hand side of the page to continue |
|                                   | to the workflow.                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 17                                | Information in Process Direct +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When progressing through the      |
|                                   | screens staff will see            |
|                                   | information with a status of:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirmed - information       |
|                                   |     previously verified about the |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   Provisional - new information |
|                                   |     updated in the claim          |
|                                   |     transaction                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Information can be added, deleted |
|                                   | or edited, as needed. See Process |
|                                   | Direct navigation, common screens |
|                                   | and functions.                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 18                                | Residency task selector + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This includes screens to confirm  |
|                                   | a customer’s legal residence      |
|                                   | status, country of citizenship,   |
|                                   | New Zealand residence status.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The system does not automatically |
|                                   | assess a customer’s residence     |
|                                   | status.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To avoid granting payments        |
|                                   | incorrectly, review all screens   |
|                                   | to make sure a customer meets the |
|                                   | residence requirements. That is:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | an Australian resident (through   |
|                                   | legal permanent residence and     |
|                                   | residing in Australia). Note: to  |
|                                   | check if a visa is permanent, see |
|                                   | Social Security Guide, 9.2, or    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the holder of a visa class        |
|                                   | permitted to work in Australia    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer must also be in      |
|                                   | Australia at the time of their    |
|                                   | claim and for the full period of  |
|                                   | the self-isolation, quarantine or |
|                                   | caring period they are claiming.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check if the customer is a legal  |
|                                   | permanent Australian resident or  |
|                                   | holds a visa that qualifies them  |
|                                   | for the Pandemic Leave Disaster   |
|                                   | Payment. Visas, and in some       |
|                                   | circumstances Australian          |
|                                   | citizenship, will show on the     |
|                                   | Legal Residence Details (RSLEG)   |
|                                   | screen. Note: for NZ citizens     |
|                                   | (Visa Sub Class Code will be 444) |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Check the New Zealand         |
|                                   |     Residence Status              |
|                                   | -   Grandfathered (GRF) is a      |
|                                   |     protected Special Category    |
|                                   |     Visa (SCV) holder and meets   |
|                                   |     the legal permanent residence |
|                                   |     aspect of being an Australian |
|                                   |     resident                      |
|                                   | -   Transitional (TRA) is a       |
|                                   |     protected SCV holder and      |
|                                   |     meets the legal permanent     |
|                                   |     residence aspect of being an  |
|                                   |     Australian resident           |
|                                   | -   Not Entitled (NOT) is a       |
|                                   |     non-protected SCV holder and  |
|                                   |     meets being the holder of a   |
|                                   |     visa class permitted to work  |
|                                   |     in Australia                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Travel documents, such as         |
|                                   | passports, will show on the       |
|                                   | Immigration Enquiry (RSIMME)      |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer has travelled since |
|                                   | 1 September 1994, movement        |
|                                   | information should show on the    |
|                                   | Immigration Advised Movements     |
|                                   | (RSIM) screen                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the arrival and departure   |
|                                   | dates for the customer on the     |
|                                   | RSIM screen to make sure the      |
|                                   | customer was in Australia for the |
|                                   | full period of the                |
|                                   | self-isolation, quarantine or     |
|                                   | caring period they are claiming   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A customer may have a successful  |
|                                   | link but no movements if they     |
|                                   | have a passport but have not      |
|                                   | travelled since 1 September 1994  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the country the customer is   |
|                                   |     currently living in is coded  |
|                                   |     on the Country of Residence   |
|                                   |     (CRES) screen, and            |
|                                   | -   steps to code relevant        |
|                                   |     information, for example,     |
|                                   |     country and date of birth are |
|                                   |     followed to prevent errors    |
|                                   |     such as S525RS. See the       |
|                                   |     Process page of Coding the    |
|                                   |     Country of Residence (CRES)   |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |     - the country a customer is   |
|                                   |     currently living in, as       |
|                                   |     provided by the customer      |
|                                   |     within their online claim,    |
|                                   |     should be uploaded into the   |
|                                   |     new claim activity            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are no details showing   |
|                                   | on the RSIM, RSLEG and/or RSIMME  |
|                                   | screens, request immigration      |
|                                   | data. On the RSIMME screen:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Request            |
|                                   |     Immigration Data button       |
|                                   | -   select Yes to continue        |
|                                   | -   once returned, the            |
|                                   |     information will show on the  |
|                                   |     relevant residence screens in |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is an error or           |
|                                   | immigration details do not match, |
|                                   | see:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Activating the Department of  |
|                                   |     Home Affairs datalink and     |
|                                   |     contingency procedures if     |
|                                   |     datalink is unavailable, or   |
|                                   | -   Referring inconsistencies in  |
|                                   |     overseas departure and        |
|                                   |     arrival information to        |
|                                   |     Centrelink International      |
|                                   |     Services (CIS)                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer meet the        |
|                                   | residence requirements and they   |
|                                   | were in Australia for the full    |
|                                   | period of self-isolation,         |
|                                   | quarantine and caring?            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, select Next to continue      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   does not meet the residence   |
|                                   |     requirements                  |
|                                   |     - The customer does not meet  |
|                                   |     the eligibility criteria      |
|                                   |     - No further customer contact |
|                                   |     is needed                     |
|                                   |     - Keep selecting Next to      |
|                                   |     continue                      |
|                                   |     - At the Claim Decision       |
|                                   |     screen, go to Step 34         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 19                                | Payment Destination Task Selector |
|                                   | (mandatory) + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Payment Destination Task      |
|                                   | Selector goes to the Payment      |
|                                   | Destination Details screen.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the bank account nominated  |
|                                   | by the customer in their claim.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the screen:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | does not need to be updated as    |
|                                   | the information matches the       |
|                                   | customer’s claim details, select  |
|                                   | Next to continue                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to Step 20                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | needs to be updated to align with |
|                                   | the details provided by the       |
|                                   | customer in their claim, consider |
|                                   | if the details are valid. If      |
|                                   | there are concerns about the      |
|                                   | validity of bank details          |
|                                   | provided, for example, multiple   |
|                                   | bank accounts used across         |
|                                   | different emergency payment       |
|                                   | claims including the Australian   |
|                                   | Government Disaster Recovery      |
|                                   | Payment and Disaster Recovery     |
|                                   | Allowance, make one attempt to    |
|                                   | contact the customer, see Table   |
|                                   | 3. Otherwise:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Edit icon [] under |
|                                   |     the Actions column            |
|                                   | -   the Change Payment            |
|                                   |     Destination Details screen    |
|                                   |     will appear                   |
|                                   | -   select the Browse button to   |
|                                   |     locate the correct BSB        |
|                                   | -   key the BSB in the search     |
|                                   |     field and select Search       |
|                                   | -   select the BSB from the       |
|                                   |     search results to return to   |
|                                   |     the Change Payment            |
|                                   |     Destination Details screen    |
|                                   | -   complete the account number   |
|                                   |     and account name details and  |
|                                   |     select Save to return to the  |
|                                   |     Payment Destination Details   |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   select Next to continue       |
|                                   | -   go to Step 20                 |
