|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If selected at the Task selectors |
|                                   | step, information in these        |
|                                   | screens should not be updated, as |
|                                   | they populate from the customer’s |
|                                   | claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue.          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 21                                | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | Task Selector (mandatory) + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment Summary (PLDP_PS) screen  |
|                                   | lists any previously granted or   |
|                                   | rejected Pandemic Leave Disaster  |
|                                   | Payment claims with a start date  |
|                                   | of on or after 18 January 2022.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key information available         |
|                                   | includes the:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   start date of the claim       |
|                                   | -   amount paid                   |
|                                   | -   event code                    |
|                                   | -   impact reason claimed         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must check this screen to   |
|                                   | determine if a customer:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | has been paid for any period that |
|                                   | overlaps with the claim they are  |
|                                   | assessing                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | has lodged a second or subsequent |
|                                   | claim and they have been paid for |
|                                   | a 7 day claiming period           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   immediately before their new  |
|                                   |     claim, or                     |
|                                   | -   that ended 7 days or less     |
|                                   |     before the start date of      |
|                                   |     their new claim               |
|                                   |     - If Yes, note this           |
|                                   |     information for later. Staff  |
|                                   |     will need to carefully check  |
|                                   |     the impact reasons to         |
|                                   |     determine next steps          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | has been paid for a different 7   |
|                                   | day claiming period on the same   |
|                                   | day as assessing this claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If Yes, note this information |
|                                   |     for later                     |
|                                   | -   If the customer meets all     |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria, 2 |
|                                   |     payments cannot be released   |
|                                   |     on the same day               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | lodged a fifth or subsequent      |
|                                   | claim and 4 claims (or more) have |
|                                   | already been paid                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If Yes, note this information |
|                                   |     for later                     |
|                                   | -   If the customer meets all     |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria:   |
|                                   |     - do not reject the claim     |
|                                   |     - follow up will be needed to |
|                                   |     request evidence from the     |
|                                   |     customer for their current    |
|                                   |     claim and all claims paid     |
|                                   |     where evidence has not been   |
|                                   |     provided                      |
|                                   | -   Note: the 4 or more claims    |
|                                   |     already paid do not have to   |
|                                   |     be paid in a row. For         |
|                                   |     example, the customer may     |
|                                   |     have lodged 8 claims. Every   |
|                                   |     second claim was paid and the |
|                                   |     other claims rejected         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Any overlapping period paid in    |
|                                   | Customer First will not show in   |
|                                   | the Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment summary screen.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Payment Summary     |
|                                   |     (PS) screen by keying ‘PS’ in |
|                                   |     the Super Key field           |
|                                   | -   Display payments for: select  |
|                                   |     FSP                           |
|                                   | -   Number of months in past: key |
|                                   |     99 months                     |
|                                   | -   If a Flexible Support Payment |
|                                   |     (FSP) payment shows, key ‘DL’ |
|                                   |     in the Super Key field to     |
|                                   |     check the customer’s Document |
|                                   |     List (DL) screen              |
|                                   | -   Review any Pandemic Leave     |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment Granted Note |
|                                   |     or DOC, CUS CLM EXG FSP DOC,  |
|                                   |     or any other Note or DOC      |
|                                   |     about this payment and to     |
|                                   |     determine if any overlapping  |
|                                   |     periods have been paid in     |
|                                   |     Customer First                |
|                                   | -   Decide if any other FSP       |
|                                   |     payments have been paid on    |
|                                   |     the same day as assessing     |
|                                   |     this claim, for example,      |
|                                   |     AGDRP. If Yes, note this      |
|                                   |     information for later, as 2   |
|                                   |     FSP payments cannot be        |
|                                   |     released on the same day      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer been paid the    |
|                                   | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | on any day of the period they     |
|                                   | have claimed?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, reject the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, if the customer has           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a second or subsequent |
|                                   |     claim (as identified above),  |
|                                   |     go to Step 22                 |
|                                   | -   not lodged a second or        |
|                                   |     subsequent claim              |
|                                   |     - Select Next to continue     |
|                                   |     - Go to Step 26               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 22                                | Second or subsequent claim -      |
|                                   | decide if it is a claim extension |
|                                   | of a previously granted claim +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Only follow this step if a        |
|                                   | customer has lodged a second or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim and an           |
|                                   | assessment has been made that     |
|                                   | they have been paid for a 7 day   |
|                                   | claiming period:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | immediately before their new      |
|                                   | claim, or                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | that ended 7 days or less before  |
|                                   | the start date of their new claim |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   for example:                  |
|                                   |     -a customer lodges a new      |
|                                   |     claim for the period 10       |
|                                   |     February to 16 February as    |
|                                   |     they tested positive with     |
|                                   |     COVID-19. Their last claim    |
|                                   |     was for the period 1 February |
|                                   |     to 7 February as they tested  |
|                                   |     positive with COVID-19. There |
|                                   |     are 2 days between the end    |
|                                   |     date and start date of these  |
|                                   |     2 claims and this would be    |
|                                   |     considered an extension       |
|                                   |     - a customer lodges a new     |
|                                   |     claim for the period 20 to 26 |
|                                   |     March as they tested positive |
|                                   |     with COVID-19. Their last     |
|                                   |     claim was for the period 5 to |
|                                   |     11 March as they tested       |
|                                   |     positive with COVID-19. There |
|                                   |     are 8 days (12 to 19 March)   |
|                                   |     before the start date and end |
|                                   |     date of these 2 claims. This  |
|                                   |     is not 7 days or less so this |
|                                   |     would not be considered an    |
|                                   |     extension                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |
|                                   | in the step above.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These claims may have the keyword |
|                                   | PLDP2NDEXT (this would have been  |
|                                   | identified at the Locating work   |
|                                   | step above).                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must decide if this claim   |
|                                   | is a claim extension of a         |
|                                   | previously granted claim.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To decide this, check the details |
|                                   | of the previously granted claim   |
|                                   | by:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   copying the Claim ID from the |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment Summary (PLDP_PS)     |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   go to the Inbox tile          |
|                                   | -   search for the Claim ID and   |
|                                   |     select the work item          |
|                                   | -   check the Claim Summary of    |
|                                   |     the previously granted claim  |
|                                   |     to decide the impact reason   |
|                                   | -   if the customer is claiming   |
|                                   |     they cared for another        |
|                                   |     person, staff must check the  |
|                                   |     name of that person           |
|                                   | -   if the customer is claiming   |
|                                   |     they or a person in their     |
|                                   |     care is a close contact,      |
|                                   |     staff must check the name of  |
|                                   |     the person who tested         |
|                                   |     positive and resulted in the  |
|                                   |     close contact                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: this claim may be for a     |
|                                   | period before a claim already     |
|                                   | granted. If granting the current  |
|                                   | claim would result in a gap of 7  |
|                                   | days or less between the end of   |
|                                   | the current claim and the start   |
|                                   | date of the already granted       |
|                                   | claim, it is considered that the  |
|                                   | claim already granted becomes an  |
|                                   | extension of the claim and is not |
|                                   | payable if the customer:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | is a close contact or caring for  |
|                                   | someone who is a close contact,   |
|                                   | and the same person who tested    |
|                                   | positive who caused the close     |
|                                   | contact status is listed in both  |
|                                   | claims                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | tested positive with COVID-19 or  |
|                                   | caring for someone who tested     |
|                                   | positive and did not answer the   |
|                                   | relevant claim extension          |
|                                   | questions                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   if this has occurred, for the |
|                                   |     claim already granted that    |
|                                   |     should not have been, see     |
|                                   |     Table 5                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Are both claims for the same      |
|                                   | impact reason?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, the impact reasons are the   |
|                                   | same. Further assessment is       |
|                                   | needed, depending on the impact   |
|                                   | reason:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Tested positive impacts. That |
|                                   |     is, the customer:             |
|                                   |     - has tested positive with    |
|                                   |     COVID-19, or                  |
|                                   |     - is caring for a child 16    |
|                                   |     years or under in their care  |
|                                   |     who has tested positive with  |
|                                   |     COVID-19, or                  |
|                                   |     - is caring for a person      |
|                                   |     other than their child who    |
|                                   |     has tested positive with      |
|                                   |     COVID-19                      |
|                                   |     - go to Step 23               |
|                                   | -   Close contact impacts. That   |
|                                   |     is, the customer is:          |
|                                   |     - a close contact of a person |
|                                   |     who has tested positive with  |
|                                   |     COVID-19 and must isolate, or |
|                                   |     - caring for a child 16 years |
|                                   |     or under in their care who    |
|                                   |     must isolate as a result of   |
|                                   |     being a close contact of a    |
|                                   |     person who has tested         |
|                                   |     positive with COVID-19, or    |
|                                   |     - caring for a person with a  |
|                                   |     disability of severe medical  |
|                                   |     condition who must isolate as |
|                                   |     a result of being a close     |
|                                   |     contact of a person who has   |
|                                   |     tested positive with COVID-19 |
|                                   |     - go to Step 24               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, the impact reasons are        |
|                                   | different. Go to step 26          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 23                                | Assessing if a claim is an        |
|                                   | extension - all ‘testing positive |
|                                   | with COVID-19’ impact reasons +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the Claim summary of the    |
|                                   | new claim to see if Extension of  |
|                                   | a period previously claimed       |
|                                   | shows:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘The period I am claiming for |
|                                   |     is an extension of an         |
|                                   |     isolation period I previously |
|                                   |     claimed for’, or              |
|                                   | -   ‘The period I am claiming for |
|                                   |     is  not  an extension of an   |
|                                   |     isolation period I previously |
|                                   |     claimed for’                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim summary of the new   |
|                                   | claim shows the customer provided |
|                                   | the response:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ‘The period I am claiming for is  |
|                                   | not an extension of an isolation  |
|                                   | period I previously claimed for’  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer is caring for |
|                                   |     a person who has tested       |
|                                   |     positive, including a child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under who has     |
|                                   |     tested positive, go to Step   |
|                                   |     24                            |
|                                   | -   If the customer has tested    |
|                                   |     positive with COVID-19, they  |
|                                   |     do not meet the eligibility   |
|                                   |     criteria, as                  |
|                                   |     - this claim is an extension  |
|                                   |     of the previously granted     |
|                                   |     claim, and                    |
|                                   |     - the customer has not        |
|                                   |     answered critical questions   |
|                                   |     to support their second or    |
|                                   |     subsequent claim              |
|                                   | -   No further customer contact   |
|                                   |     is needed                     |
|                                   | -   Isolation details in Process  |
|                                   |     Direct may auto-populate a No |
|                                   |     response next to the question |
|                                   |     ‘Is this 7 day claim period   |
|                                   |     an extension of a previously  |
|                                   |     claimed period of             |
|                                   |     isolation/caring?’            |
|                                   | -   Staff must change this to Yes |
|                                   | -   After changing to Yes, a      |
|                                   |     question will appear          |
|                                   |     ‘Customer has evidence of     |
|                                   |     need for continuing their     |
|                                   |     isolation/caring past the     |
|                                   |     initial 7 days?’              |
|                                   | -   Select No, as this will make  |
|                                   |     sure a ‘Reject’ outcome       |
|                                   |     populates in the Claim        |
|                                   |     Decision screen               |
|                                   | -   Keep selecting Next to        |
|                                   |     continue                      |
|                                   | -   At the Claim Decision screen, |
|                                   |     go to Step 34                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ‘The period I am claiming for is  |
|                                   | an extension of an isolation      |
|                                   | period I previously claimed for’, |
|                                   | go to Step 25                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 24                                | Assessing if a claim is an        |
|                                   | extension - all ‘close contact’   |
|                                   | and ‘caring’ impact reasons +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The response to Extension of a    |
|                                   | period previously claimed         |
|                                   | question will determine if the    |
|                                   | customer is asked the question    |
|                                   | ‘has there been a change in the   |
|                                   | impact reason’.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Even if the Extension of a period |
|                                   | previously claimed question has   |
|                                   | not been asked or answered by the |
|                                   | customer, staff must complete an  |
|                                   | assessment on if                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   there has been a change in    |
|                                   |     the impact reason, and        |
|                                   | -   the current claim is an       |
|                                   |     extension of the previously   |
|                                   |     granted claim                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff do this by carefully        |
|                                   | checking the following            |
|                                   | information in the customer’s     |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Impact information, and       |
|                                   | -   Name of the person the        |
|                                   |     customer is caring for (if    |
|                                   |     relevant), and                |
|                                   | -   Name of the person who tested |
|                                   |     positive and caused the close |
|                                   |     contact status of the         |
|                                   |     customer or the person the    |
|                                   |     customer is caring for        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Examples of when the current      |
|                                   | claim is not an extension of the  |
|                                   | previously granted claim + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The caring reason has changed |
|                                   |     from caring for their child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under, to caring  |
|                                   |     for a person with a           |
|                                   |     disability or severe medical  |
|                                   |     condition and the names of    |
|                                   |     the people being cared for    |
|                                   |     have changed, or              |
|                                   | -   In the previous claim they    |
|                                   |     were caring for their child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under and now     |
|                                   |     they are claiming for their   |
|                                   |     other child and the names of  |
|                                   |     the children cared for have   |
|                                   |     changed, or                   |
|                                   | -   In the previous claim they    |
|                                   |     were caring for their child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under and now     |
|                                   |     they are claiming for the     |
|                                   |     same child and the name of    |
|                                   |     the person who made their     |
|                                   |     child a close contact (the    |
|                                   |     person who tested positive)   |
|                                   |     has changed                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, see Table 5 in          |
|                                   | Resources or contact Technical    |
|                                   | Peer Support.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Keep assessing the customer’s     |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Under Impact reason/Isolation     |
|                                   | details, if the question ‘Impact  |
|                                   | reason has changed since previous |
|                                   | 7 day claim period?’ shows:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A No response may auto        |
|                                   |     populate next to this         |
|                                   |     question                      |
|                                   | -   Staff must change this to Yes |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reminder: there is an additional  |
|                                   | process to follow if a customer   |
|                                   | has lodged a fifth or subsequent  |
|                                   | claim. Continue assessing the     |
|                                   | claim. A later step will advise   |
|                                   | when to see Table 7               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 26                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Examples of when the current      |
|                                   | claim is an extension of the      |
|                                   | previously granted claim + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The caring reason has changed |
|                                   |     from caring for a child 16    |
|                                   |     years or under, to caring for |
|                                   |     a person with a disability or |
|                                   |     severe medical condition.     |
|                                   |     However, the names of the     |
|                                   |     people being cared for are    |
|                                   |     the same, or                  |
|                                   | -   In the previous claim, they   |
|                                   |     were caring for their child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under and now     |
|                                   |     they are claiming for their   |
|                                   |     other child. However, the     |
|                                   |     names of the children being   |
|                                   |     cared for are the same        |
|                                   | -   In the previous claim, they   |
|                                   |     were caring for their child   |
|                                   |     16 years or under and now     |
|                                   |     they are claiming for the     |
|                                   |     same child. However, the      |
|                                   |     names of the person who made  |
|                                   |     their child a close contact   |
|                                   |     (the person who tested        |
|                                   |     positive) are the same        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For more examples, see Table 5 in |
|                                   | Resources. If more help is needed |
|                                   | contact Technical Peer Support.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer does not meet the    |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, as:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   this claim is an extension of |
|                                   |     the previously granted claim, |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   | -   the customer cannot be paid   |
|                                   |     for extensions of close       |
|                                   |     contact impacts               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No further customer contact is    |
|                                   | needed                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Under Impact reason/Isolation     |
|                                   | details, if the question ‘Impact  |
|                                   | reason has changed since previous |
|                                   | 7 day claim period?’ shows:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A Yes response may auto       |
|                                   |     populate next to this         |
|                                   |     question                      |
|                                   | -   Staff must change this to No, |
|                                   |     as this will make sure a      |
|                                   |     ‘Reject’ outcome populates in |
|                                   |     the Claim Decision screen     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Keep selecting Next to continue   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | At the Claim Decision screen, go  |
|                                   | to Step 34                        |

| 25                                | Previously granted claim was      |

| 27                                | Eligibility Confirmation screen + |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | information from the customer’s   |
|                                   | online claim or Assisted Customer |
|                                   | Claim (ACC).                      |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   navigates to the Claim        |

|                                   |     eligible), or                 |
|                                   | -   continues through the         |
|                                   |     workflow                      |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | claim, staff assess the claim to  |
|                                   | be eligible, but unexpectedly go  |

|                                   | the Reject button is              |

|                                   | Previous button to return to this |
|                                   | page to review and correct any    |
|                                   | information. Do not select the    |
|                                   | Back button, as this will take    |
|                                   | staff out of the workflow.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim navigates to the     |

| 29                                | Impact Reason screen + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This shows why the customer is    |
|                                   | claiming the Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must check address details  |
|                                   | in a Claim Summary when a         |
|                                   | customer is claiming as they:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | are caring for a person with a    |
|                                   | disability or severe medical      |
|                                   | condition who must self-isolate   |
|                                   | or quarantine, as they are close  |
|                                   | contact of a person who has       |
|                                   | tested positive with COVID-19, or |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | are the close contact of a person |
|                                   | who has tested positive with      |
|                                   | COVID-19 and they live in the     |
|                                   | same household as that person     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: address details do not  |
|                                   |     need to match if a customer   |
|                                   |     has indicated in their claim  |
|                                   |     that they ‘have spent 4 hours |
|                                   |     or more in the same household |
|                                   |     as a positive COVID-19 person |
|                                   |     during their infectious       |
|                                   |     period’                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In these instances, the address   |
|                                   | of the customer must match the    |
|                                   | address of the person with a      |
|                                   | disability or severe medical      |
|                                   | condition, or the address of the  |
|                                   | person the customer lives with    |
|                                   | who has tested positive with      |
|                                   | COVID-19.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the addresses in the           |
|                                   | customer's claim do not match,    |
|                                   | reject the claim.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, go to Step 30          |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 31                                | Liquid Assets + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Liquid Assets screen captures |
|                                   | information from the customer’s   |
|                                   | claim about their:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Savings                       |
|                                   | -   Bonds and debentures          |
|                                   | -   Money loaned to others, or    |
|                                   | -   Other liquid assets           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This information also shows in    |
|                                   | the My finances - Savings section |
|                                   | of the Claim Summary.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A Total will show at the bottom   |
|                                   | of the Liquid Assets screen.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The system will automatically     |
|                                   | calculate the Customer share (%). |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must check if the value of  |
|                                   | assets listed meets the           |
|                                   | definition of liquid assets for   |
|                                   | the Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment. See Liquid assets.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If assets are being included that |
|                                   | should not be and the Total is    |
|                                   | $10,000 or more, the system will  |
|                                   | reject the claim.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer has included  |
|                                   | the exact same account details    |
|                                   | and balance more than once, only  |
|                                   | consider the one entry.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Total is:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | $10,000 or more and all assets    |
|                                   | listed meet the definition of     |
|                                   | liquid assets for the Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The customer does not meet    |
|                                   |     the eligibility criteria      |
|                                   | -   No further customer contact   |
|                                   |     is needed                     |
|                                   | -   Select Next to continue       |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 32                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | $10,000 or more, assets included  |
|                                   | do not meet the definition of     |
|                                   | liquid assets for the Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment, and total |
|                                   | of liquid assets should be less   |
|                                   | than $10,000 ($9,999 or less)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer meets all     |
|                                   |     other eligibility criteria,   |
|                                   |     do not allow the system to    |
|                                   |     reject the claim              |
|                                   | -   Note: The system will         |
|                                   |     automatically default to      |
|                                   |     reject the claim based on     |
|                                   |     reading the liquid assets as  |
|                                   |     being over $10,000. Contact   |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support, who   |
|                                   |     will                          |
|                                   |     - review the claim, and       |
|                                   |     - decide if the customer has  |
|                                   |     a total liquid asset balance  |
|                                   |     below $10,000, and            |
|                                   |     - if appropriate, authorise   |
|                                   |     changing the status of the    |
|                                   |     claim to allow a grant        |
|                                   |     outcome                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Less than $10,000 ($9,999.99 or   |
|                                   | less)                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Next to continue       |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 32                 |

|                                   | 2022 to lodge a claim.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This is a system issue. Note: |

|                                   |     via Roxy quoting 'Claim       |
|                                   |     lodged outside 14 days'. If   |
|                                   |     this has not been done, do    |
|                                   |     this now                      |

|                                   |     reasons for late claims       |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     that meets all other          |

| 33                                | Dates in Claim Summary - system   |
|                                   | issue + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer meet all other  |
|                                   | eligibility criteria and at the   |

|                                   | period’                           |

|                                   |     time I’ll provide care for    |

|                                   |     provided for this person from |
|                                   |     27 April to 3 May 2022’ and   |
|                                   |     ‘Start date of the 7 day      |

|                                   |     from 6 May 2022.’ 27 April to |
|                                   |     3 May 2022 falls entirely     |
|                                   |     before 6 May 2022             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   | Support.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This is a system issue. Note: |
|                                   |     the View Claim Summary step   |
|                                   |     advised to raise an incident  |
|                                   |     via Roxy quoting              |
|                                   |     - 'Entire period of care      |
|                                   |     occurs before the start date  |
|                                   |     of the 7 day claim period'    |
|                                   | -   If this has not been done, do |
|                                   |     this now                      |
|                                   | -   Attempt to contact the        |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   Go to Table 3                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the claim assessed is a    |
|                                   |     fifth or subsequent claim     |
|                                   |     that meets all other          |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria but      |
|                                   |     cannot be granted until       |
|                                   |     evidence is provided by the   |
|                                   |     customer for their current    |
|                                   |     and previous claims paid, go  |
|                                   |     to Table 7                    |
|                                   | -   Otherwise, go to Step 34      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 34                                | Claim Decision screen + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If, at the Review record and      |
|                                   | Notes/DOCs step (above) staff     |
|                                   | identified customer contact is    |
|                                   | needed to discuss claims          |
|                                   | withdrawn within the last 14 days |
|                                   | and the customer meets all other  |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, go to Table |
|                                   | 3.                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim Decision screen will    |
|                                   | recommend an outcome based on the |
|                                   | information provided in the       |
|                                   | claim.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The outcome may be manually       |
|                                   | over-ridden as needed. Staff      |
|                                   | should review the information in  |
|                                   | the claim (particularly the       |
|                                   | Eligibility Confirmation screen)  |
|                                   | if the outcome is not what was    |
|                                   | expected. To do this, select the  |
|                                   | Previous button. Do not select    |
|                                   | the Back button, as this will     |
|                                   | take staff out of the workflow.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer meets all           |
|                                   | eligibility criteria, a FRDCHK    |
|                                   | keyword is not attached to the    |
|                                   | claim and there are no concerns   |
|                                   | about the validity of the claim,  |
|                                   | if previous claims granted and    |
|                                   | paid were investigated due to     |
|                                   | concerns about fraud:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   staff do not need to take any |
|                                   |     action on these claims        |
|                                   | -   a specialist fraud team will  |
|                                   |     investigate and action these  |
|                                   |     claims as needed              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: staff should have           |
|                                   | identified the FRDCHK keyword at  |
|                                   | the Review keywords step and      |
|                                   | unassigned the claim.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Grant recommendation - customer   |
|                                   | contact or further checks are     |
|                                   | needed + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This means a Service Officer has  |
|                                   | assessed the customer meets all   |
|                                   | eligibility criteria however,     |
|                                   | before a grant outcome can be     |
|                                   | finalised:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   further contact with the      |
|                                   |     customer is needed by         |
|                                   |     appropriately trained staff,  |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   appropriately trained staff   |
|                                   |     need to further check the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record to make     |
|                                   |     sure payment can be made      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer needs to be       |
|                                   | contacted as they have uploaded   |
|                                   | identity documents since lodging  |
|                                   | their phone claim (Assisted       |
|                                   | Customer Claim), contact the      |
|                                   | customer (identified in the       |
|                                   | Transaction Summary screen step   |
|                                   | above).                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 35 if:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the customer has a payment    |
|                                   |     nominee and has no FSP        |
|                                   |     payment in the Payment        |
|                                   |     Destination Summary (PAS)     |
|                                   |     screen (identified in the     |
|                                   |     Processing the claim step) or |
|                                   | -   an ISP, DAP or PPL trained    |
|                                   |     staff member needs to contact |
|                                   |     the customer (identified in   |
|                                   |     the Pending, NCL, ASS, SUS,   |
|                                   |     DAP, PPL step above)          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact Technical Peer Support    |
|                                   | and see the Escalating claims     |
|                                   | table if the customer is          |
|                                   | receiving the Home Equity Access  |
|                                   | Scheme and has an ISP status of   |
|                                   | (primary benefit)/(status), for   |
|                                   | example, AGE/CZR – PLS            |
|                                   | (identified in the Check ISP step |
|                                   | above).                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Grant Recommendation - no further |
|                                   | customer contact or checks are    |
|                                   | needed + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the information in the claim   |
|                                   | indicates the customer is         |
|                                   | eligible:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the Payment Component to    |
|                                   | make sure the information is      |
|                                   | correct. See Payment rates        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If not, staff should speak    |
|                                   |     with their Pandemic Leave     |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment Service      |
|                                   |     Support Officer (SSO) or team |
|                                   |     leader to have this possible  |
|                                   |     system issue/error            |
|                                   |     investigated, as these        |
|                                   |     details should match in all   |
|                                   |     instances                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the claim information and  |
|                                   | make any corrections as needed.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next to continue the       |
|                                   | workflow.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 36                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reject Recommendation + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the information in the claim   |
|                                   | indicates the customer is not     |
|                                   | eligible for payment the Reject   |
|                                   | Reason field and Additional       |
|                                   | rejection details (if needed)     |
|                                   | will pre-populate based on the    |
|                                   | information within the claim. If  |
|                                   | the steps above indicate a        |
|                                   | customer’s claim can be rejected  |
|                                   | without further customer contact, |
|                                   | continue with this process.       |
|                                   | Otherwise, go to Rejecting claims |
|                                   | to make one attempt to contact    |
|                                   | the customer then return to this  |
|                                   | step.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: there is a process for      |
|                                   | staff to follow if they cannot    |
|                                   | make outbound calls.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim is being rejected    |
|                                   | due to concerns about fraud, see  |
|                                   | Table 8.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If one genuine attempt to contact |
|                                   | the customer has been made, (or   |
|                                   | is not needed), and the claim is  |
|                                   | to be rejected:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the appropriate Reject |
|                                   |     reason from the drop down     |
|                                   | -   select Next to continue the   |
|                                   |     workflow                      |
|                                   | -   go to Step 36                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 35                                | Payment nominee + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Documents icon         |
|                                   | [Documents] from the menu bar.    |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |

|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images.        |

|                                   |     the PAS screen (this should   |
|                                   |     have been identified in the   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the error X032AS - No       |

|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section by selecting    |
|                                   | the Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To help the next Service      |
|                                   |     Officer, clearly document why |
|                                   |     the customer meets all other  |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria and that |
|                                   |     a staff member with !FFAP     |
|                                   |     access needs to complete the  |
|                                   |     claim processing              |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Close document         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Keyword icon from the  |
|                                   | menu bar                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Add (+) icon.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key NOM in the search field or    |
|                                   | scroll through the list to find   |
|                                   | it                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the NOM keyword. The       |
|                                   | keyword will save                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Inbox in Process Direct |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |

|                                   | -   Select the transaction from   |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   | -   Select Unassign at the bottom |
|                                   |     of the screen to unassign the |
|                                   |     claim with the Reason of      |
|                                   |     Second contact attempt        |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will return NOM claims to    |
|                                   | the allocation pool to be         |
|                                   | reallocated to a trained staff    |
|                                   | member                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not put the claim on hold      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff with !FFAP access:          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   | -   See Table 6 to finalise the   |
|                                   |     claim in the !FFAP screen     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Pending, assessed or suspended    |
|                                   | ISP, or status of DAP/NCL,        |

|                                   | more ...                          |

|                                   | menu bar, then annotate the       |

|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section by selecting    |
|                                   | the Annotate hyperlink            |

|                                   | -   Clearly document why the      |
|                                   |     customer meets all other      |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria and that |
|                                   |     a staff member trained in the |

|                                   |     to discuss their              |
|                                   |     circumstances                 |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | menu bar                          |

|                                   | search field or scroll through    |
|                                   | the list to find it               |

|                                   | keyword will save                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Inbox in Process Direct |
|                                   | to Unassign the claim             |
