| 36                                | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | for a different period or another |
|                                   | Flexible Support Payment (FSP)    |
|                                   | payment + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | At the Pandemic Leave Disaster    |
|                                   | Payment Task Selectors            |
|                                   | (mandatory) step, did staff       |
|                                   | identify if the customer has been |
|                                   | paid, on the same day as          |
|                                   | assessing this claim:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | for a different 7 day Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | period                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | any other Flexible Support        |
|                                   | Payment (FSP) payments, for       |
|                                   | example, AGDRP                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Stop                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   2 payments of Pandemic Leave  |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment/FSP cannot   |
|                                   |     be released on the same day   |
|                                   |     for any customer              |
|                                   | -   Staff can complete an         |
|                                   |     assessment of the additional  |
|                                   |     payment, but cannot finalise  |
|                                   |     it with a grant outcome       |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section by |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Clearly document why the      |
|                                   |     customer’s claim cannot be    |
|                                   |     granted and paid today        |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Status icon        |
|                                   |     [Status] from the menu bar    |
|                                   | -   Select the Edit [] icon to    |
|                                   |     change the status             |
|                                   | -   The Change Status screen will |
|                                   |     show, select On Hold from the |
|                                   |     Status drop down              |
|                                   | -   Select Delay FSP Release as   |
|                                   |     the On Hold Reason            |
|                                   | -   If processing the claim       |
|                                   |     - on a weekday (Monday to     |
|                                   |     Friday), set the due to date  |
|                                   |     as the next day using the     |
|                                   |     calendar icon                 |
|                                   |     - on a weekend (Saturday or   |
|                                   |     Sunday), set the due to date  |
|                                   |     as the following Tuesday      |
|                                   |     using the calendar icon.      |
|                                   |     Note: payment for claims      |
|                                   |     processed on a Saturday or    |
|                                   |     Sunday are not delivered      |
|                                   |     until the following Monday,   |
|                                   |     setting the date to the       |
|                                   |     following Tuesday avoids      |
|                                   |     multiple payments on the one  |
|                                   |     day.                          |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer’s record. This   |
|                                   |     will go back to the Process   |
|                                   |     Direct Landing Page. Note:    |
|                                   |     staff should not have the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record open in     |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors         |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 44                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 37                 |

| 37                                | Assessing the claim + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once all screens in the workflow  |
|                                   | have been reviewed, staff will    |
|                                   | return to the Warning and Errors  |
|                                   | (SWE) screen.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Assess to send the claim   |
|                                   | information to ISIS for           |
|                                   | assessment. Note: it may take     |
|                                   | several seconds for the           |
|                                   | information to be sent, assessed  |
|                                   | and the result to be returned.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Any errors returned from ISIS     |

|                                   | review and action.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do any errors show?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 38            |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 40             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 38                                | Errors, Warnings and Roxy + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Errors must be resolved before    |
|                                   | the claim can be finalised.       |
|                                   | Warnings should be considered but |
|                                   | do not need to disappear before   |
|                                   | the claim can be finalised.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If staff receive an error they do |
|                                   | not know how to resolve, use the  |
|                                   | Roxy Digital assistant for help.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For more details about warnings   |
|                                   | and errors, see Using Digital     |
|                                   | Assistant Roxy in Process Direct. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the E027FY error shows on the  |
|                                   | SWE screen, if the customer is    |
|                                   | subscribed, issue a pre-call      |
|                                   | notification (SMS) to the         |
|                                   | customer between 8:00 am and 8:00 |
|                                   | pm using the customer's local     |
|                                   | time to let them know a Service   |
|                                   | Officer will call them today from |
|                                   | a private number.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer to discuss   |
|                                   | their family income estimate      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Contact successful            |
|                                   |     - Ask the customer to give    |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   |     - Families trained staff -    |
|                                   |     update the customer’s record  |
|                                   |     with an income estimate for   |
|                                   |     the current financial year    |
|                                   |     - Not Families trained        |
|                                   |     staff - contact the F&P       |
|                                   |     Payment Queries TPS via       |
|                                   |     Services Australia Workspace  |
|                                   |     or 177111 for help            |
|                                   | -   Contact unsuccessful, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 39                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After fixing any errors, select   |
|                                   | Assess again to go to the         |
|                                   | Entitlements (ELD) screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if Roxy does not have the   |
|                                   | information needed to resolve an  |
|                                   | error, provide feedback using the |
|                                   | Thumbs Down option. This will     |
|                                   | help Roxy learn and help others   |
|                                   | in the future.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If staff receive an error warning |
|                                   | that the customer has             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a payment nominee (error X032AS - |
|                                   | No Payment Destination, please    |
|                                   | update via PA screen), return to  |
|                                   | the Payment nominee step in Table |
|                                   | 1                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | reached the Maximum Amount        |
|                                   | (Mainframe Error: E044FF – Update |
|                                   | Error – Component amount exceed   |
|                                   | balance), this means the customer |
|                                   | has been paid for 6 or more       |
|                                   | claims under the same event code, |
|                                   | and the system will not allow a   |
|                                   | seventh or subsequent claim to be |
|                                   | paid. If the customer             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   has not been asked to provide |
|                                   |     evidence to support their     |
|                                   |     claim, do not reject the      |
|                                   |     claim. To ask for evidence,   |
|                                   |     see Table 7                   |
|                                   | -   has been asked to provide     |
|                                   |     evidence to support their     |
|                                   |     claim, check if the evidence  |
|                                   |     supports their claim and      |
|                                   |     previous claims paid (if this |
|                                   |     evidence is also needed). See |
|                                   |     Table 7                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once all errors have been         |
|                                   | resolved, select Assess again to  |
|                                   | send the updated information to   |
|                                   | ISIS for assessment.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 39                                | E027FY error - customer contact   |
|                                   | was not successful + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |
|                                   | in the Assess claim step above.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Place the claim on hold           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select [] to change the       |
|                                   |     status                        |
|                                   | -   The Change Status screen will |
|                                   |     show. Select On Hold from the |

|                                   | -   Select Customer to provide    |
|                                   |     information as the On Hold    |
|                                   |     Reason                        |
|                                   | -   Set the due to date. For      |
|                                   |     customers with:               |

|                                   |     date from the calendar 28     |
|                                   |     days + an additional 2        |
|                                   |     working days                  |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 28     |
|                                   |     days and allow extra time for |
|                                   |     mail delivery, see Time       |
|                                   |     allowed to respond            |
|                                   | -   If the error message ‘OnHold  |

|                                   |     OnHold Expiry Date). This     |
|                                   |     will allow the date nominated |
|                                   |     in the calendar to be         |
|                                   |     selected                      |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update the Progress of Claim Note |
|                                   | on the DL screen under Notes      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Annotate               |
|                                   | -   Record details of why the     |
|                                   |     claim has been placed on hold |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will return to the   |
|                                   | Process Direct landing page       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First. Note: staff       |
|                                   | should not have the customer’s    |
|                                   | record open in Customer First and |
|                                   | Process Direct at the same time,  |
|                                   | as this can cause errors          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Search Workspace: key Family   |
|                                   | Income and Choices Workflow then  |
|                                   | select Search                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source and Receipt details screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Families Income    |
|                                   |     and Choices Workflow          |
|                                   | -   Tick box, select Follow up    |
|                                   |     income estimate               |
|                                   | -   Source: from the dropdown,    |
|                                   |     select Request For Income     |
|                                   |     Details                       |
|                                   | -   Document Storage: from the    |
|                                   |     dropdown, select No Document  |
|                                   |     involved                      |
|                                   | -   Contact by: from the          |
|                                   |     dropdown, select CSO          |
|                                   | -   Select Continue               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Follow up Income Estimate screen  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select letters or form(s) you |
|                                   |     wish to send: from the        |
|                                   |     dropdown, select FA078 -      |
|                                   |     Confirmation of Family Income |
|                                   | -   Would you like to set a       |
|                                   |     review?: Select No            |
|                                   | -   What is the reason for        |
|                                   |     issuing form(s)/letter?: From |
|                                   |     the dropdown, select Estimate |
|                                   |     not complete                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer Discussion screen        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Declaration: tick Customer    |
|                                   |     Acknowledges. Disregard the   |
|                                   |     requirement to read the       |
|                                   |     declaration as the customer   |
|                                   |     is not on the phone           |
|                                   | -   Select Continue               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note pages entries from pages     |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Include additional            |
|                                   |     information or notes below in |
|                                   |     the box provided              |
|                                   | -   Select Continue               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Assessment Confirmation screen    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Continue with assessment?:    |
|                                   |     select Continue               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Assessment results (AR) screen    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select:                       |
|                                   |     - the Finalise radio button,  |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   |     - Continue                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 40                                | Entitlement screen + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entitlements (ELD) screen     |
|                                   | will show the results of the      |
|                                   | assessment and where the claim is |
|                                   | to be granted, the payment amount |
|                                   | to be sent to the customer.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the payment/decision is        |
|                                   | correct, select Finish.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 41                                | Finalise + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A Finalise DOC or Note window     |
|                                   | will show.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check the information.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim is to be:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   rejected, clearly document    |
|                                   |     the reason why                |
|                                   | -   granted due to information in |
|                                   |     a CSO CLM EXG PLDP review ACC |
|                                   |     run DOC, document that no     |
|                                   |     further review can be         |
|                                   |     requested by the customer     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if the decision needs to be |
|                                   | changed, select the Do Not        |
|                                   | Finalise button. This will:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   return to the beginning of    |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   | -   allow staff to go through     |
|                                   |     each screen                   |
|                                   | -   allow updates to be made and  |
|                                   |     the decision to be changed,   |
|                                   |     as needed                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Finalise button to     |
|                                   | complete the claim.               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 42                                | Document list/notes and Payment   |
|                                   | Summary + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the claim is finalised,      |
|                                   | finalisation notes will appear on |
|                                   | the Document list/notes screen in |
|                                   | Process Direct. Staff can         |
|                                   | navigate to this screen by keying |
|                                   | ‘DL’ in the Super Key field.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a claim has been granted,      |
|                                   | staff can also check the Payment  |
|                                   | Summary (PS) screen by keying     |
|                                   | ‘PS’ in the Super Key field to    |
|                                   | confirm the claim has finalised   |
|                                   | as intended.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the decision Note and       |
|                                   | payment will also show in the     |
|                                   | corresponding screens in Customer |
|                                   | First.                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 43                                | Claim rejected after request for  |
|                                   | evidence to support fifth or      |
|                                   | subsequent claim and previous     |
|                                   | claims paid was not provided +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |
|                                   | in Table 7 Step 12                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, a minimum standards      |
|                                   |     ACTDOC must be created with   |
|                                   |     debt information for previous |
|                                   |     claims paid. Go to Table 5    |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 44             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 44                                | Open EM252 form or related DOCs + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After a claim is processed in     |
|                                   | Process Direct, any DOCs that are |
|                                   | ‘open’ on the customer’s record   |
|                                   | will show.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |
|                                   | uploaded as part of a Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | (such as identity documents,      |
|                                   | evidence of testing positive with |
|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is an ‘open’ Claim for   |
|                                   | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | form (EM252), this means an EM252 |
|                                   | needs to be assessed and a        |
|                                   | decision finalised. See           |
|                                   | Processing Pandemic Leave         |
|                                   | Disaster Payment claims in        |
|                                   | Customer First.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 45                                | If a claim cannot proceed or be   |
|                                   | finalised - Open EM252 form or    |
|                                   | related DOCs + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a claim cannot proceed or be   |
|                                   | finalised, select the Documents   |
|                                   | icon [Documents] from the menu    |
|                                   | bar.                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |
|                                   | uploaded as part of a Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | (such as identity documents,      |
|                                   | evidence of testing positive with |
|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has lodged a      |
|                                   | Claim for Pandemic Leave Disaster |
|                                   | Payment form (EM252) that has not |
|                                   | been finalised, see Processing    |
|                                   | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | claims in Customer First.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Rejecting claims

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 2: Process to follow if a customer’s claim is to be rejected. For
help with any steps, contact Technical Peer Support.

If a customer contacts the agency after a claim has been rejected to
provide more information or to advise they disagree with a decision
made, they can request an explanation of the decision. A formal review
cannot be undertaken. Do not try to process a new claim to change the
decision.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Customer contact requirements     |
|                                   | when rejecting a claim + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not all reasons for rejection     |
|                                   | will need contact with the        |
|                                   | customer.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer's claim is being  |
|                                   | rejected for one of the following |
|                                   | reasons no customer contact is    |
|                                   | needed:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not residentially qualified       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claims with the keyword FRDREJ    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not in Australia at time of claim |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not in Australia for the full     |
|                                   | period of the self-isolation,     |
|                                   | quarantine or caring period they  |
|                                   | are claiming                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Liquid Assets over $10k           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have leave entitlements which     |
|                                   | cover the full 7 day period the   |
|                                   | customer is claiming              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Less than 17 years of age         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Receiving one of the following    |
|                                   | payments during their claim       |
|                                   | period:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an income support payment     |
|                                   |     (including zero rate)         |
|                                   | -   ABSTUDY Living Allowance      |
|                                   | -   Dad and Partner Pay (DAP)     |
|                                   | -   Parental Leave Pay (PPL)      |
|                                   | -   ACT COVID-19 Hardship Payment |
|                                   | -   NSW Test and Isolate support  |
|                                   |     payment                       |
|                                   | -   South Australian COVID-19     |
|                                   |     Cluster Isolation Payment     |
|                                   | -   Tasmanian Test and Isolate    |
|                                   |     Grant                         |
|                                   | -   Tasmanian Pandemic Isolation  |
|                                   |     Grant Assistance              |
|                                   | -   Victorian COVID-19 Test       |
|                                   |     Isolation Payment             |
|                                   | -   Victorian Sick Pay Guarantee  |
|                                   | -   Western Australian COVID-19   |
|                                   |     Test Isolation Payment        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Lodged a second or subsequent     |
|                                   | claim and answered in their claim |
|                                   | ‘The period I am claiming for is  |
|                                   | not an extension of an isolation  |
|                                   | period I previously claimed for’  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer has not provided         |
|                                   | evidence requested to support a   |
|                                   | fifth or subsequent claim to be   |
|                                   | paid                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Intelligence and Investigation    |
|                                   | Branch assessment indicating      |
|                                   | claim is not valid                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer has not provided         |
|                                   | evidence requested to support     |
|                                   | their claim (including late       |
|                                   | claim)                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer lodged a fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim, and             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an RFI letter was sent        |
|                                   |     requesting evidence to        |
|                                   |     support that claim, and       |
|                                   | -   they withdrew that fifth or   |
|                                   |     subsequent claim or that      |
|                                   |     claim was rejected as the     |
|                                   |     customer ‘Failed to Provide   |
|                                   |     Information’ (FPI) and        |
|                                   | -   they then lodged a new fifth  |
|                                   |     or subsequent claim without   |
|                                   |     the evidence previously       |
|                                   |     requested                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | As no customer contact is needed, |
|                                   | go to Table 1 Step 34 to finalise |
|                                   | (reject) the claim in Process     |
|                                   | Direct using the rejection reason |
|                                   | Do not meet conditions of         |
|                                   | payment.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer contacts      |
|                                   | after a claim has been rejected,  |
|                                   | to give more details or to say    |
|                                   | they disagree with a decision     |
|                                   | made, they can request an         |
|                                   | explanation of the decision. A    |
|                                   | formal review cannot be           |
|                                   | undertaken. Do not try to process |
|                                   | a new claim to change the         |
|                                   | decision, this includes           |
|                                   | processing a new claim made for   |
|                                   | the same period.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer's claim is being  |
|                                   | rejected for any other reason,    |
|                                   | staff must make one genuine       |
|                                   | attempt to contact the customer.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Can an outbound call to customers |
|                                   | be made (some staff cannot make   |
|                                   | outbound calls)?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Outbound contact cannot be made + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Process Direct:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword CONREQ into   |
|                                   |     the search field or scroll    |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the CONREQ keyword.    |
|                                   |     The keyword will save         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Documents icon         |
|                                   | [Documents] from the menu bar.    |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |
|                                   | uploaded as part of a Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | (such as identity documents,      |
|                                   | evidence of testing positive with |
|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Inbox in Process Direct |
|                                   | to Unassign the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   | -   Select Multi Select           |
|                                   | -   Select the transaction from   |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   | -   Select Unassign at the bottom |
|                                   |     of the screen to unassign the |
|                                   |     claim with the Reason of      |
|                                   |     Second contact attempt        |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page.      |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First, go to the      |
|                                   | customer's record and run the     |
|                                   | Fast Note workflow:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Auto Text, use         |
|                                   |     Emergency > Pandemic Leave    |
|                                   |     Disaster > PLDP Customer      |
|                                   |     Contact Req'd                 |
|                                   | -   Select Confirm                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Answer all questions/prompts      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the Fast Note.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the CONREQ keyword will     |
|                                   | allow the claim to be allocated   |
|                                   | to a staff member who can make    |
|                                   | outbound calls.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Contact attempt + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   Decide if the customer can    |
|                                   |     qualify under any other       |
|                                   |     criteria or if details in     |
|                                   |     their claim can be updated    |
|                                   |     based on the new information. |
|                                   |     This includes where the       |
|                                   |     customer can upload evidence  |
|                                   |     now to support their claim    |
|                                   |     and they can do this while on |
|                                   |     the phone for staff to assess |
|                                   |     during the call               |
|                                   |     - if they can, return to      |
|                                   |     Table 1 to make any required  |
|                                   |     updates and to grant the      |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct.      |
|                                   |     Note: the Impact Reason       |
|                                   |     screen can be updated if the  |
|                                   |     customer qualifies under      |
|                                   |     other criteria                |
|                                   | -   If the customer is still not  |
|                                   |     eligible, including being     |
|                                   |     unable to upload evidence now |
|                                   |     to support their claim while  |
|                                   |     on the phone, tell them       |
|                                   |     - why they do not meet        |
|                                   |     requirements for the payment  |
|                                   |     - that they can request an    |
|                                   |     explanation of the decision   |
|                                   |     - they will get a letter      |
|                                   |     confirming the decision and   |
|                                   |     advising of their right to    |
|                                   |     request an explanation        |
|                                   |     - Return the Claim Decision   |
|                                   |     screen (Table 1 Step 34) to   |
|                                   |     finalise (reject) the claim   |
|                                   |     in Process Direct             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/notes section   |
|                                   |     by selecting the Annotate     |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Clearly document why customer |
|                                   |     contact is needed             |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select Next until the Claim   |
|                                   |     Decision screen is reached    |
|                                   | -   Go to Table 1 Step 34 to      |
|                                   |     finalise (reject) the claim   |
|                                   |     in Process Direct             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer contacts the  |
|                                   | agency after a claim has been     |
|                                   | rejected to provide more          |
|                                   | information or to advise they     |
|                                   | disagree with a decision made,    |
|                                   | they can request an explanation   |
|                                   | of the decision. A formal review  |
|                                   | cannot be undertaken. Do not try  |
|                                   | to process a new claim to change  |
|                                   | the decision.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Asking for information or evidence

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 3: Process if more details are needed to finalise a claim and the
customer is not on the phone. For help with any steps, contact Technical
Peer Support.

Only follow this process when advised to from Table1.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Attempting to contact the         |
|                                   | customer + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If contacting a customer to       |
|                                   | request evidence for a fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim and claims       |
|                                   | already paid, see Table 7.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before contacting a customer to   |
|                                   | ask for more information or       |
|                                   | evidence to support their claim,  |
|                                   | make sure                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   all pre-claim checks in Table |
|                                   |     1 have been completed         |
|                                   | -   the customer meets all other  |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria for      |
|                                   |     payment, and                  |
|                                   | -   all information needed from   |
|                                   |     the customer to support their |
|                                   |     claim is discussed in the one |
|                                   |     contact                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: statutory declarations will |
|                                   | not be accepted as evidence to    |
|                                   | support a claim.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | One genuine attempt to contact    |
|                                   | the customer must be made.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Can an outbound call to customers |
|                                   | be made? Note: some staff cannot  |
|                                   | make outbound calls.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Outbound contact cannot be made + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Process Direct:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword CONREQ into   |
|                                   |     the search field or scroll    |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the CONREQ keyword The |
|                                   |     keyword will save             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Documents icon         |
|                                   | [Documents] from the menu bar.    |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |
|                                   | uploaded as part of a Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | (such as identity documents,      |
|                                   | evidence of testing positive with |
|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Inbox in Process Direct |
|                                   | to Unassign the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   | -   Select Multi Select           |
|                                   | -   Select the transaction from   |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   | -   Select Unassign at the bottom |
|                                   |     of the screen to unassign the |
|                                   |     claim with the Reason of      |
|                                   |     Second contact attempt        |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page.      |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First, go to the      |
|                                   | customer's record and run the     |
|                                   | Fast Note workflow:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Auto Text, use         |
|                                   |     Emergency > Pandemic Leave    |
|                                   |     Disaster > PLDP Customer      |
|                                   |     Contact Req'd                 |
|                                   | -   Select Confirm                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Answer all questions/prompts      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the Fast Note.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the CONREQ keyword will     |
|                                   | allow the claim to be allocated   |
|                                   | to a staff member who can make    |
|                                   | outbound calls.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Contact attempt + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer and ask for  |
|                                   | the information.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   If the call was to verify     |
|                                   |     identity documents that were  |
|                                   |     uploaded since a phone claim  |
|                                   |     (Assisted Customer Claim),    |
|                                   |     see identity requirements     |
|                                   |     (this should have been        |
|                                   |     identified at the Claim       |
|                                   |     Decision screen step in Table |
|                                   |     1)                            |
|                                   | -   If the call was to discuss a  |
|                                   |     late claim, as the customer   |
|                                   |     did not lodge their claim     |
|                                   |     within 14 days from and       |
|                                   |     including the first day of    |
|                                   |     their 7 day claiming period,  |
|                                   |     determine if the customer has |
|                                   |     a special reason for the late |
|                                   |     claim. See Common definitions |
|                                   |     when considering late claims. |
|                                   |     Go to Step 4                  |
|                                   | -   If the call was to discuss    |
|                                   |     claims withdrawn in the last  |
|                                   |     14 days, this would have been |
|                                   |     identified in the Review      |
|                                   |     record and Notes/DOCs step in |
|                                   |     Table 1. Go to Step 5         |
|                                   | -   If the call was for any other |
|                                   |     reason, depending on the      |
|                                   |     discussion with the customer: |
|                                   |     - return to Table 1 Step 34   |
|                                   |     to finalise (grant or reject) |
|                                   |     the claim, or                 |
|                                   |     - if the customer advises     |
|                                   |     they have evidence to support |
|                                   |     their claim, go to Step 6     |
|                                   |     - if there are still concerns |
|                                   |     the customer’s claim may be   |
|                                   |     fraudulent, including payment |
|                                   |     destination details provided, |
|                                   |     see Table 8                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/notes section   |
|                                   |     by selecting the Annotate     |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Clearly document why customer |
|                                   |     contact is needed             |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   If there are concerns the     |
|                                   |     customer’s claim may be       |
|                                   |     fraudulent, see Table 8       |
|                                   | -   Otherwise, return to Table 1  |
|                                   |     Step 34 to finalise (reject)  |
|                                   |     the claim in Process Direct   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer contacts the  |
|                                   | agency after a claim has been     |
|                                   | rejected to provide more          |
|                                   | information or to advise they     |
|                                   | disagree with a decision made,    |
|                                   | they can request an explanation   |
|                                   | of the decision. A formal review  |
|                                   | cannot be undertaken. Do not try  |
|                                   | to process a new claim to change  |
|                                   | the decision.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Customer contact to discuss a     |
|                                   | late claim was successful + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer meet all of the |
|                                   | following?                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Meets one of the special      |
|                                   |     reasons for a late claim, and |
|                                   | -   Can upload evidence within 7  |
|                                   |     days, and                     |
|                                   | -   Meets all other eligibility   |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if there are concerns about |
|                                   | the validity of the customer’s    |
|                                   | claim, see Table 8. Do not grant  |
|                                   | the claim.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, to go Step 6             |
|                                   | -   No, reject the claim          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Different circumstances to        |
|                                   | previous withdrawn claims in the  |
|                                   | last 14 days + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer advises different   |
|                                   | details to their previously       |
|                                   | withdrawn claim/s, and is         |
|                                   | advising different details for    |
|                                   | the purposes of completing a      |
|                                   | claim, this would have been       |
|                                   | identified in the Review record   |
|                                   | and Notes/DOCs step in Table 1.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must determine:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the reason for the changed    |
|                                   |     information                   |
|                                   | -   if evidence is needed to      |
|                                   |     assess the claim              |
|                                   | -   if the claim should be        |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask the customer why they had to  |
|                                   | withdraw and re-lodge their       |
|                                   | claim/s. For example, were they   |
|                                   | trying to add new information or  |
|                                   | having difficulty with the online |
|                                   | claim?                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ask more probing and open-ended   |
|                                   | questions to verify the details   |
|                                   | they are providing in their new   |
|                                   | claim and what they declared in   |
|                                   | their previous claims             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not:                       |
|                                   |     - give the customer answers   |
|                                   |     to questions                  |
|                                   |     - prompt them for correct     |
|                                   |     answers, or                   |
|                                   |     - include details they can    |
|                                   |     use to frame their responses  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Record the outcome of the         |
|                                   | discussion in the Progress of     |
|                                   | claim Note on the DL screen under |
|                                   | the Document list/note section    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not use the term ‘fraud’   |
|                                   |     in the Note                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer’s change in       |
|                                   | circumstances sound valid and no  |
|                                   | more evidence is needed to        |
|                                   | support their current claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   include reasons why in the    |
|                                   |     Progress of claim Note        |
|                                   | -   return to Table 1 Step 34 to  |
|                                   |     finalise (grant) the claim in |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are irregularities in    |
|                                   | the customer’s information, and   |
|                                   | there are concerns about the      |
|                                   | validity of the claim, request    |
|                                   | the customer upload documents via |
|                                   | the Upload Documents Service so   |
|                                   | their claim can be assessed       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For evidence customers are    |
|                                   |     asked to keep to support      |
|                                   |     their claim as Services       |
|                                   |     Australia may ask for it      |
|                                   |     later, see Evidence in the    |
|                                   |     Background page of Processing |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claims in Process     |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   | -   Note: statutory declarations  |
|                                   |     will not be accepted as       |
|                                   |     evidence to support a claim   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer advises they will |
|                                   | upload the necessary documents    |
