|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Tell the customer their claim     |
|                                   | will not be assessed until they   |
|                                   | submit the requested evidence.    |
|                                   | They should do this within 7      |
|                                   | days, otherwise they will receive |
|                                   | notification from the agency      |
|                                   | their claim is ineligible         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Encourage the customer to upload  |
|                                   | documents via the Upload          |
|                                   | Documents Service the same day to |
|                                   | minimise delays in processing     |
|                                   | their claim                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Include in the Progress of Claim  |
|                                   | Note evidence the customer was    |
|                                   | asked to provide                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To place the claim On Hold    |
|                                   |     for 7 days                    |
|                                   |     - Select the Status icon from |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   |     - Select the Edit [] icon to  |
|                                   |     change the status             |
|                                   |     - The Change Status screen    |
|                                   |     will show. Select On Hold     |
|                                   |     from the Status drop down     |
|                                   |     - Select Customer to provide  |
|                                   |     information as the On Hold    |
|                                   |     Reason                        |
|                                   |     - Set the due to date to 7    |
|                                   |     days from today’s date using  |
|                                   |     the calendar icon             |
|                                   |     - Select Save                 |
|                                   |     - Select the Keyword icon     |
|                                   |     from the menu bar             |
|                                   |     - Select the Add (+) icon     |
|                                   |     - Key the keyword EVD in the  |
|                                   |     search field or scroll        |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   |     - Select the EVD keyword. The |
|                                   |     keyword will save             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there are concerns about the   |
|                                   | validity of the claim, go to      |
|                                   | Table 8                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, procedure ends here    |
|                                   | until evidence is uploaded or the |
|                                   | claim comes off hold, then go to  |
|                                   | Step 7                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer advises they will |
|                                   | not provide any evidence and      |
|                                   | there is no valid reason for not  |
|                                   | providing evidence                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Tell the customer: ‘Your      |
|                                   |     claim cannot be granted as    |
|                                   |     eligibility cannot be         |
|                                   |     established’                  |
|                                   | -   Do not use the term ‘fraud’   |
|                                   |     when speaking with the        |
|                                   |     customer or when updating     |
|                                   |     their record                  |
|                                   | -   Include in the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note why the claim is   |
|                                   |     being rejected                |
|                                   | -   To reject the claim with no   |
|                                   |     further customer contact and  |
|                                   |     report suspected fraud, go to |
|                                   |     Table 8                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Customer has evidence they can    |
|                                   | upload to support their claim +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This would have been identified   |
|                                   | at Step 3 or 4 above.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: statutory declarations will |
|                                   | not be accepted as evidence to    |
|                                   | support a claim.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Tell the customer:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   they need to upload evidence  |
|                                   |     within 7 days. Encourage the  |
|                                   |     customer to upload documents  |
|                                   |     via the Upload Documents      |
|                                   |     Service the same day to       |
|                                   |     minimise delays in processing |
|                                   |     their claim                   |
|                                   | -   once evidence is received,    |
|                                   |     the claim will be reviewed    |
|                                   |     and assessed                  |
|                                   | -   if evidence that supports     |
|                                   |     their late claim is not       |
|                                   |     uploaded within 7 days (this  |
|                                   |     includes no evidence uploaded |
|                                   |     or insufficient evidence      |
|                                   |     uploaded to support their     |
|                                   |     claim), they will not meet    |
|                                   |     the eligibility requirements  |
|                                   |     for payment and their claim   |
|                                   |     will be ineligible            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Under Customer and Activity       |
|                                   | Information, check the Links      |
|                                   | Summary (LS) under Circumstance   |
|                                   | Data in the menu bar.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer has a payment |
|                                   |     nominee, the NOM line on LS   |
|                                   |     will have NOP coded in the    |
|                                   |     ‘To’ column.                  |
|                                   | -   If the customer has a payment |
|                                   |     nominee tell the customer     |
|                                   |     those details will be used to |
|                                   |     deliver their payment         |
|                                   | -   If the customer asks to       |
|                                   |     cancel a voluntary            |
|                                   |     arrangement, (customers       |
|                                   |     cannot cancel an involuntary  |
|                                   |     arrangement), see Cancelling  |
|                                   |     a nominee arrangement. For    |
|                                   |     help, contact Technical Peer  |
|                                   |     Support                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Notes icon from the    |
|                                   | menu bar, then annotate the       |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section by selecting    |
|                                   | the Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Clearly document:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   what was discussed with the   |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   evidence they have been asked |
|                                   |     to provide within 7 days      |
|                                   | -   they have been advised their  |
|                                   |     claim will be ineligible if   |
|                                   |     evidence that supports their  |
|                                   |     claim is not uploaded within  |
|                                   |     7 days (this includes no      |
|                                   |     evidence uploaded or          |
|                                   |     insufficient evidence         |
|                                   |     uploaded to support their     |
|                                   |     claim)                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Put the claim on hold for 7 days. |
|                                   | To place a claim on hold:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Status icon from   |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Edit [] icon to    |
|                                   |     change the status             |
|                                   | -   The Change Status screen will |
|                                   |     show, select On Hold from the |
|                                   |     Status drop down              |
|                                   | -   Select the Customer to        |
|                                   |     provide information as the On |
|                                   |     Hold Reason                   |
|                                   | -   Set the due to date to 7 days |
|                                   |     from today’s date using the   |
|                                   |     calendar icon                 |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword EVD in the    |
|                                   |     search field or scroll        |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the EVD keyword. The   |
|                                   |     keyword will save             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here until the     |
|                                   | claim comes off hold, then go to  |
|                                   | Step 7                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Claim comes off hold after        |
|                                   | customer was asked to provide     |
|                                   | evidence + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Evidence would have been          |
|                                   | requested as per step 3, 4 or 5   |
|                                   | above                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must review:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   all claim details to make     |
|                                   |     sure the customer meets the   |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria see      |
|                                   |     Table 1, and                  |
|                                   | -   any evidence uploaded to make |
|                                   |     sure this supports the        |
|                                   |     customer’s claim (including   |
|                                   |     special reasons for a late    |
|                                   |     claim where applicable).      |
|                                   |     Note: if a customer has not   |
|                                   |     uploaded evidence as          |
|                                   |     requested, or evidence        |
|                                   |     uploaded does not support a   |
|                                   |     claim (including special      |
|                                   |     reasons for a late claim      |
|                                   |     where applicable), contact is |
|                                   |     not needed before rejecting   |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update the Progress of claim Note |
|                                   | with why the claim is to be       |
|                                   | granted or rejected.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To finalise (grant or reject) the |
|                                   | claim, go to Table 1 Step 34.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Escalating claims

Table 4: Process to follow when Technical Peer Support is seeking advice
from the Level 2 Helpdesk.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Escalation + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the escalation refers to:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   multiple claims for the same  |
|                                   |     period, go to Step 3          |
|                                   | -   customer has reached the      |
|                                   |     maximum amount and a seventh  |
|                                   |     or subsequent claim can be    |
|                                   |     paid (do not follow this      |
|                                   |     process until all steps in    |
|                                   |     Table 7 have been completed), |
|                                   |     go to Step 2                  |
|                                   | -   any other policy or payment   |
|                                   |     processing query, go to Step  |
|                                   |     2                             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Put claim on hold + Read more ... |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section by |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Clearly document why the      |
|                                   |     claim cannot be finalised     |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Put the claim on hold for 28  |
|                                   |     days                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To place a claim on hold:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Status icon from   |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Edit [] icon to    |
|                                   |     change the status             |
|                                   | -   The Change Status screen will |
|                                   |     show, select On Hold from the |
|                                   |     Status drop down              |
|                                   | -   Select the Awaiting Policy    |
|                                   |     Advice as the On Hold Reason  |
|                                   | -   Set the due to date to 28     |
|                                   |     days from today’s date using  |
|                                   |     the calendar icon             |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon.      |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword PE in the     |
|                                   |     search field or scroll        |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the PE keyword. The    |
|                                   |     keyword will save             |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     the transaction. This will go |
|                                   |     back to the Process Direct    |
|                                   |     Landing Page                  |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 3                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Complete Payment Query Template + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the Payment Query        |
|                                   | Template with the claim details.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Multiple claims for the same  |
|                                   |     period, procedure ends here   |
|                                   | -   Any other policy or payment   |
|                                   |     processing query, go to Step  |
|                                   |     4                             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Level 2 Helpdesk gives advice +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Where required, the Level 2       |
|                                   | Helpdesk sends an email:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   advising what action to take  |
|                                   | -   to the original sender from   |
|                                   |     Technical Peer Support        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Level 2 Helpdesk may    |
|                                   | need to resolve issues and        |
|                                   | finalise claims in some           |
|                                   | instances, and may not contact    |
|                                   | the original sender from          |
|                                   | Technical Peer Support            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Technical Peer Support advises    |
|                                   | Service Officer + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Technical Peer Support contacts   |
|                                   | the relevant Service Officer to   |
|                                   | finalise the claim.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Advice provided by the Level 2    |
|                                   | Helpdesk must be documented on    |
|                                   | the customer’s record.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Finalise claim + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the customer’s claim.    |
|                                   | See Table 1.                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment was incorrectly paid

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

If a payment has been issued incorrectly and the payment was made by NPP
or immediate payment, this cannot be stopped by the Stop Payment process
with help from the ICT Service Desk. Do not follow steps in Payment of
arrears after reassessment.

Table 5: Process to follow when the Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment was
incorrectly paid. For help with any steps, contact Technical Peer
Support.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Payment should not have been      |
|                                   | granted + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the customer's record and  |
|                                   | the decision to pay Pandemic      |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the customer eligible to get  |
|                                   | the payment?                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 3              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Payment correct + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Process Direct.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key ‘DL’ in the Super Key field.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the payment made correctly    |
|                                   | and is the payment amount         |
|                                   | correct?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Annotate the Pandemic Leave   |
|                                   |     Claim - Grant Summary Note by |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Record the reason why the     |
|                                   |     claim was correctly granted   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the incorrect event code   |
|                                   |     was paid but the correct      |
|                                   |     amount was paid, annotate the |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Claim - Grant  |
|                                   |     Summary Note by selecting the |
|                                   |     Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |     - Do not pay the customer     |
|                                   |     under the event code they     |
|                                   |     should have been paid under   |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   If the incorrect event code   |
|                                   |     and incorrect amount were     |
|                                   |     paid, go to Step 3            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Incorrect amount was paid         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer was underpaid + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer was paid $450 but   |
|                                   | should have been paid $750:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The customer can request an   |
|                                   |     explanation of the decision.  |
|                                   |     A formal review cannot be     |
|                                   |     undertaken. Do not try to     |
|                                   |     process a new claim to change |
|                                   |     the decision                  |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer was overpaid or should   |
|                                   | not have been paid + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer should not have     |
|                                   | been paid, or was paid $750 and   |
|                                   | should have been paid $450:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Process Direct.            |
|                                   | -   Key ‘DL’ in the Super Key     |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   | -   Annotate all relevant         |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Claim - Grant  |
|                                   |     Summary DOCs by selecting the |
|                                   |     Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   | -   Record the reason why the     |
|                                   |     customer was overpaid         |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer’s record. Note:  |
|                                   |     staff should not have the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record open in     |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors.        |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   | -   Create a minimum standards    |
|                                   |     ACTDOC using the              |
|                                   |     Callback/ACTDOC guided        |
|                                   |     procedure                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To create the minimum standards   |
|                                   | ACTDOC                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Search Workspace field     |
|                                   | type: Callback/ACTDOC then select |
|                                   | search                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on the Callback/ACTDOC      |
|                                   | hyperlink                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the ACTDOC as follows:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Who contacted: from the drop  |
|                                   |     down select Customer Service  |
|                                   |     Officer                       |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: from the drop |
|                                   |     down select Emergency         |
|                                   |     Exgratia                      |
|                                   | -   Type: from the drop down      |
|                                   |     select ACTDOC                 |
|                                   | -   Category: from the drop down  |
|                                   |     select Debt Raising           |
|                                   | -   Contact Method: from the drop |
|                                   |     down select Internal (to      |
|                                   |     Centrelink)                   |
|                                   | -   Channel: from the drop down   |
|                                   |     select Internal Channels      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate Document Content  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Document Content, add the      |
|                                   | reason the customer was overpaid. |
|                                   | Include the details of how the    |
|                                   | overpayment occurred, such as:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the customer only lost 19     |
|                                   |     hours, not 20, or             |
|                                   | -   incorrect Event selected for  |
|                                   |     customer paid $750 when they  |
|                                   |     stated they lost X hours      |
|                                   | -   customer did not provide the  |
|                                   |     requested evidence to support |
|                                   |     the payment of a {ENTER CLAIM |
|                                   |     NUMBER, for example, fifth    |
|                                   |     claim, sixth claim} and       |
|                                   |     {ENTER NUMBER OF CLAIMS       |
|                                   |     ALREADY PAID, for example, 4  |
|                                   |     claims, 5 claims} have        |
|                                   |     already been paid.            |
|                                   |     Overpayment to be raised for  |
|                                   |     all previous claims paid for  |
|                                   |     self-isolation, quarantine or |
|                                   |     caring periods that start on  |
|                                   |     or after 18 January 2022      |
|                                   | -   customer lodged an ACC and    |
|                                   |     did not provide the required  |
|                                   |     identity documents in the     |
|                                   |     requested timeframe           |
|                                   |     - Note: a manual review with  |
|                                   |     the keyword POIPLDP may have  |
|                                   |     been allocated. See Table 3   |
|                                   |     in Pandemic Leave Disaster    |
|                                   |     Payment - Assisted Customer   |
|                                   |     Claims and Table 10           |
|                                   |     This manual review should be  |
|                                   |     cancelled. To cancel the      |
|                                   |     manual review:                |
|                                   |     - Key AL in the Next field    |
|                                   |     and press [Enter]             |
|                                   |     - Select the manual review    |
|                                   |     with the keyword POIPLDP      |
|                                   |     - Select cancel and continue  |
|                                   |     - Select Yes - cancel the     |
|                                   |     Activity and continue         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finish at the top left     |
|                                   | corner of the screen              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Activity List (AL)      |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the ACTDOC activity        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select O Transfer the activity to |
|                                   | another site or region            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Regional Office enter: XWA     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In New Keywords add keyword:      |
|                                   | PLDPDEBT                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

!FFAP Screen - processing claims

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 6: how to finalise claims where there is a payment nominee and the
X032AS - No Payment Destination, please update via PA screen error shows
in Process Direct, stopping the claim from finalising (that is, the
customer has not previously claimed an FSP payment).

Staff must not follow this process unless assigned one of the above
claim types and have the required access to the !FFAP screen.

Only staff with access to Flexible Support Payment FFAP will be
allocated these claims to finalise.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Customers with nominee            |
|                                   | arrangements + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Payments must be issued in        |
|                                   | Customer First using the !FFAP    |
|                                   | screen when the X032AS - No       |
|                                   | Payment Destination, please       |
|                                   | update via PA screen error shows  |
|                                   | in Process Direct, stopping the   |
|                                   | claim from finalising (that is,   |
|                                   | the customer has not previously   |
|                                   | claimed an FSP payment). This     |
|                                   | requires access to the FSPFFAP    |
|                                   | resource.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | allocated a claim started by      |
|                                   | another Service Officer who did   |
|                                   | not have access to the !FFAP      |
|                                   | screen, go to Step 2              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | continuing a claim from Process   |
|                                   | Direct and the Service Officer    |
|                                   | has access to the !FFAP screen.   |
|                                   | If the claim is to be:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   granted, to ‘handover’ the    |
|                                   |     claim and finalise it in      |
|                                   |     Customer First, go to Step 4  |
|                                   | -   rejected, go to Step 3        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Review the claim + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the claim details in       |
|                                   | Process Direct and any documents  |
|                                   | related to the claim to determine |
|                                   | if the customer is eligible. See  |
|                                   | Table 1                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim is to be             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   granted, to ‘handover’ the    |
|                                   |     claim and finalise it in      |
|                                   |     Customer First, go to Step 4  |
|                                   | -   rejected, go to Step 3        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Contact attempt + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer's claim is being  |
|                                   | rejected for one of the following |
|                                   | reasons:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not residentially qualified       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not in Australia at time of claim |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Not in Australia for the full     |
|                                   | period of the self-isolation,     |
|                                   | quarantine or caring period they  |
|                                   | are claiming                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Liquid Assets over $10k           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have leave entitlements which     |
|                                   | cover the full 7 day period the   |
|                                   | customer is claiming              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Less than 17 years of age         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Receiving one of the following    |
|                                   | payments during their claim       |
|                                   | period:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an income support payment     |
|                                   |     (including zero rate)         |
|                                   | -   ABSTUDY Living Allowance      |
|                                   | -   Dad and Partner Pay (DAP)     |
|                                   | -   Parental Leave Pay (PPL)      |
|                                   | -   ACT COVID-19 Hardship Payment |
|                                   | -   NSW Test and Isolate support  |
|                                   |     payment                       |
|                                   | -   South Australian COVID-19     |
|                                   |     Cluster Isolation Payment     |
|                                   | -   Tasmanian Test and Isolate    |
|                                   |     Grant                         |
|                                   | -   Tasmanian Pandemic Isolation  |
|                                   |     Grant Assistance              |
|                                   | -   Victorian COVID-19 Test       |
|                                   |     Isolation Payment             |
|                                   | -   Victorian Sick Pay Guarantee  |
|                                   | -   Western Australian COVID-19   |
|                                   |     Test Isolation Payment        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Lodged a second or subsequent     |
|                                   | claim and answered in their claim |
|                                   | ‘The period I am claiming for is  |
|                                   | not an extension of an isolation  |
|                                   | period I previously claimed for’  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer has not provided         |
|                                   | evidence requested to support a   |
|                                   | fifth or subsequent claim to be   |
|                                   | paid                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Intelligence and Investigation    |
|                                   | Branch assessment indicating      |
|                                   | claim is not valid                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer has not provided         |
|                                   | evidence requested to support     |
|                                   | their claim                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a customer lodged a fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim, and             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an RFI letter was sent        |
|                                   |     requesting evidence to        |
|                                   |     support that claim, and       |
|                                   | -   they withdrew that fifth or   |
|                                   |     subsequent claim or that      |
|                                   |     claim was rejected as the     |
|                                   |     customer ‘Failed to Provide   |
|                                   |     Information’ (FPI) and        |
|                                   | -   they then lodged a new fifth  |
|                                   |     or subsequent claim without   |
|                                   |     the evidence previously       |
|                                   |     requested                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No customer contact is needed.    |
|                                   | 'Handover' the claim and finalise |
|                                   | it in Customer First, go to Step  |
|                                   | 4.                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim is to be rejected    |
|                                   | for any other reason, if the      |
|                                   | customer is subscribed, issue a   |
|                                   | pre-call notification (SMS only)  |
|                                   | between 8:00 am and 8:00 pm using |
|                                   | the customer's local time, to let |
|                                   | them know a Service Officer will  |
|                                   | call them today from a private    |
|                                   | number.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Ask the customer to give      |
|                                   |     Proof of Record Ownership     |
|                                   |     (PoRO). Do not give hints or  |
|                                   |     prompts that help the         |
|                                   |     customer answer the PoRO      |
|                                   |     questions                     |
|                                   | -   Decide if the customer can    |
|                                   |     qualify under any other       |
|                                   |     criteria                      |
|                                   |     - if they can, to ‘handover’  |
|                                   |     the claim and finalise it in  |
|                                   |     Customer First, go to Step 4  |
|                                   | -   If the customer is still not  |
|                                   |     eligible, tell them           |
|                                   |     - why they do not meet        |
|                                   |     requirements for the payment  |
|                                   |     - they can request an         |
|                                   |     explanation of the decision   |
|                                   |     - they will get a letter      |
|                                   |     confirming the decision and   |
|                                   |     advising of their right to    |
|                                   |     request and explanation       |
|                                   |     - to ‘handover’ the claim and |
|                                   |     finalise it in Customer       |
|                                   |     First, go to Step 4           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section by |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Clearly document why customer |
|                                   |     contact is needed             |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   The claim is to be rejected   |
|                                   | -   To ‘handover’ the claim and   |
|                                   |     finalise it in Customer       |
|                                   |     First, go to Step 4           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Handover to Customer First + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Once the customer’s claim has     |
|                                   | been reviewed and a decision can  |

|                                   | First                             |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | select the Reason: FUA – Function |

|                                   | automatically place the claim in  |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will go back to the  |
|                                   | Process Direct Landing Page.      |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |

|                                   | -   rejected, go to Step 6        |

| 5                                 | !FFAP screen in Customer First -  |
