|                                   | Act 1997 (delete what does not    |
|                                   | apply)                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer has been contacted to    |
|                                   | advise of the rejection reason?   |
|                                   | <Yes/No>                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Appeal rights provided to the     |
|                                   | customer? <Yes/No>                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | NOTE: all claim information is    |
|                                   | contained within the claim in     |
|                                   | Process Direct. For more          |
|                                   | information, refer to this claim. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer contacts the  |
|                                   | agency after a claim has been     |
|                                   | rejected to provide more          |
|                                   | information or to advise they     |
|                                   | disagree with a decision made,    |
|                                   | they can request an explanation   |
|                                   | of the decision. A formal review  |
|                                   | cannot be undertaken. Do not try  |
|                                   | to process a new claim to change  |
|                                   | the decision                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 8.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Update Progress of Claim Note in  |
|                                   | Process Direct + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First. Staff should not  |
|                                   | have the customer’s record open   |
|                                   | in Customer First and Process     |
|                                   | Direct at the same time, as this  |
|                                   | can cause errors                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s claim in |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
|                                   | -   Select the Notes icon from    |
|                                   |     the menu bar, then annotate   |
|                                   |     the Progress of Claim Note on |
|                                   |     the DL screen under the       |
|                                   |     Document list/note section by |
|                                   |     selecting the Annotate        |
|                                   |     hyperlink                     |
|                                   | -   Add the following “Claim      |
|                                   |     finalised via !FFAP in CF due |
|                                   |     to system limitations”.       |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Fifth or subsequent claim – request evidence

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 7: where evidence needs to be requested and provided by a customer
before their fifth or subsequent claim can be granted. This would have
been identified in Table 1

Note: subsequent means any claim lodged after a fifth claim that was
previously lodged.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Requesting evidence or claim has  |
|                                   | come off hold + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process applies when a       |
|                                   | customer lodges a fifth or        |
|                                   | subsequent claim that appears to  |
|                                   | meet the eligibility criteria and |
|                                   | 4 or more claims have already     |
|                                   | been granted and paid.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: subsequent means any claim  |
|                                   | lodged after a fifth claim that   |
|                                   | was previously lodged.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The 4 or more claims already paid |
|                                   | do not have to be paid in a row.  |
|                                   | For example, the customer may     |
|                                   | have lodged 8 claims. Every       |
|                                   | second claim was paid and the     |
|                                   | other claims rejected.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not refer to the number of     |
|                                   | claims lodged.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: a claim can be rejected     |
|                                   | with no further customer contact  |
|                                   | if                                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a customer lodged a fifth or      |
|                                   | subsequent claim, and             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | an RFI letter was sent requesting |
|                                   | evidence to support that claim,   |
|                                   | and                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they withdrew that fifth or       |
|                                   | subsequent claim or that claim    |
|                                   | was rejected as the customer      |
|                                   | ‘Failed to Provide Information’   |
|                                   | (FPI) and                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they then lodged a new fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim without the      |
|                                   | evidence previously requested     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To reject the claim using the |
|                                   |     rejection reason Do not meet  |
|                                   |     conditions of payment, see    |
|                                   |     the Claim Decision step in    |
|                                   |     Table 1                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Continue to assess the claim if   |
|                                   | the customer has:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a fifth or subsequent  |
|                                   |     claim after a previous        |
|                                   |     withdrawal, and               |
|                                   | -   has provided all evidence     |
|                                   |     previously requested to       |
|                                   |     support previous claims paid  |
|                                   |     and their current claim. See  |
|                                   |     Table 1                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Statutory declarations will not   |
|                                   | be accepted as evidence to        |
|                                   | support a claim.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If evidence to support a fifth or |
|                                   | subsequent claim and previous     |
|                                   | claims paid have:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | not yet been requested, go to     |
|                                   | Step 2                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | been requested and staff have     |
|                                   | been allocated a work item that   |
|                                   | has come off hold. If the hold    |
|                                   | period ending is:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   due to a request for          |
|                                   |     information for a fifth or    |
|                                   |     subsequent claim ending, go   |
|                                   |     to Step 9                     |
|                                   | -   not due to a request for      |
|                                   |     information for a fifth or    |
|                                   |     subsequent claim ending       |
|                                   |     - Check the claim to          |
|                                   |     determine if any updates or   |
|                                   |     actions are needed            |
|                                   |     - If the claim cannot be      |
|                                   |     finalised as the customer has |
|                                   |     not been provided 14 days to  |
|                                   |     respond, plus more time as    |
|                                   |     per agency standards, place   |
|                                   |     the claim on hold again for   |
|                                   |     the remainder of the initial  |
|                                   |     hold period. For example, if  |
|                                   |     a customer was given 22 days  |
|                                   |     to respond and only 2 days    |
|                                   |     have passed since the request |
|                                   |     for information was made,     |
|                                   |     hold the claim for another 20 |
|                                   |     days. To hold the claim, go   |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   |     - If the claim can be         |
|                                   |     finalised as the customer has |
|                                   |     been provided 14 days to      |
|                                   |     respond plus more time as per |
|                                   |     agency standards, go to Step  |
|                                   |     9                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | been requested and staff          |
|                                   | identify:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the review date for the       |
|                                   |     Request for Information (RFI) |
|                                   |     letter sent has expired, and  |
|                                   | -   no action has been taken to   |
|                                   |     determine next steps          |
|                                   | -   go to Step 9                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Check if claim was lodged using   |
|                                   | Assisted Customer Claim (ACC) and |
|                                   | customer advised Request For      |
|                                   | Information (RFI) will be sent +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Transaction Summary (TS)   |
|                                   | screen, if the ‘Channel’ of the   |
|                                   | claim shows as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | WEB CHANNEL, this is an online    |
|                                   | claim lodged by a customer        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘Submitted by’ will show the  |
|                                   |     customer’s CRN                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | INTERNAL this is a phone claim    |
|                                   | lodged using ACC                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim shows as INTERNAL,   |
|                                   | key ‘DL‘ in the Super Key field   |
|                                   | to go the customer’s Document     |
|                                   | List (DL) screen.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there a DOC titled PLDP fifth  |
|                                   | or subsequent that relates to the |
|                                   | customers claim? Note: this DOC   |
|                                   | should have been created if       |
|                                   | needed during a phone claim       |
|                                   | (Assisted Customer Claim).        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, customer contact is not      |
|                                   | needed, as this DOC means the     |
|                                   | customer:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a phone claim          |
|                                   |     (Assisted Customer Claim)     |
|                                   | -   was told the evidence they    |
|                                   |     need to provide, and          |
|                                   | -   was told they will receive a  |
|                                   |     letter that confirms the      |
|                                   |     evidence they need to provide |
|                                   | -   go to Step 4                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, customer contact is needed,   |
|                                   | for staff who:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   cannot make outbound contact  |
|                                   |     go to Step 3                  |
|                                   | -   can make outbound contact, go |
|                                   |     to Step 4                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Outbound contact cannot be made + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Process Direct:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword ‘CONREQ’ into |
|                                   |     the search field or scroll    |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the CONREQ keyword The |
|                                   |     keyword will save             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Documents icon         |
|                                   | [Documents] from the menu bar.    |
|                                   | Any ‘open’ DOCs or evidence       |
|                                   | uploaded as part of a Pandemic    |
|                                   | Leave Disaster Payment claim      |
|                                   | (such as identity documents,      |
|                                   | evidence of testing positive with |
|                                   | COVID-19) should be completed.    |
|                                   | See Table 1 in Viewing Centrelink |
|                                   | customers’ digital images         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Inbox in Process Direct |
|                                   | to Unassign the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   In Main Category select WLM   |
|                                   |     Worklist from the drop down   |
|                                   |     options                       |
|                                   |     - Select Multi Select         |
|                                   |     - Select the transaction from |
|                                   |     the list                      |
|                                   |     - Select Unassign at the      |
|                                   |     bottom of the screen to       |
|                                   |     unassign the claim with the   |
|                                   |     Reason of Second contact      |
|                                   |     attempt required              |
|                                   |     - Select Submit               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. Note: staff should not    |
|                                   | have the customer’s record open   |
|                                   | in Customer First and Process     |
|                                   | Direct at the same time, as this  |
|                                   | can cause errors.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First, go to the      |
|                                   | customer's record and run Fast    |
|                                   | Note - select Auto Text, use      |
|                                   | Emergency > Pandemic Leave        |
|                                   | Disaster > PLDP Customer Contact  |
|                                   | Req'd                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Confirm                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Answer all questions/prompts      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the Fast Note               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the CONREQ keyword will     |
|                                   | allow the claim to be allocated   |
|                                   | to a staff member who can make    |
|                                   | outbound calls to                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   contact the customer, and     |
|                                   | -   send the required Request for |
|                                   |     Information (RFI) letter      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Send RFI letter + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Send an RFI letter in Process     |
|                                   | Direct requesting evidence for    |
|                                   | all claim periods paid where the  |
|                                   | customer has not yet provided     |
|                                   | evidence, and evidence to support |
|                                   | the current claim.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Request all evidence needed in    |
|                                   | the one RFI letter.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: if a customer has already   |
|                                   | been asked to provide evidence    |
|                                   | for previous claims and has not   |
|                                   | done this within 14 days, there   |
|                                   | is no need to ask for it again.   |
|                                   | This might happen if a:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   previous claim has been       |
|                                   |     rejected                      |
|                                   | -   debt raising ACTDOC has been  |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If any of the above happen, only  |
|                                   | ask for evidence of claims that   |
|                                   | have not been requested yet.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: a claim can be rejected     |
|                                   | with no further customer contact  |
|                                   | if:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a customer lodged a fifth or      |
|                                   | subsequent claim, and             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | an RFI letter was sent requesting |
|                                   | evidence to support that claim,   |
|                                   | and                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they withdrew that fifth or       |
|                                   | subsequent claim or that claim    |
|                                   | was rejected as the customer      |
|                                   | ‘Failed to Provide Information’   |
|                                   | (FPI) and                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | they then lodged a new fifth or   |
|                                   | subsequent claim without the      |
|                                   | evidence previously requested     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To reject the claim using the |
|                                   |     rejection reason Do not meet  |
|                                   |     conditions of payment, see    |
|                                   |     the Claim Decision step in    |
|                                   |     Table 1                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Continue to assess the claim if   |
|                                   | the customer has:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a fifth or subsequent  |
|                                   |     claim after a previous        |
|                                   |     withdrawal, and               |
|                                   | -   has provided all evidence     |
|                                   |     previously requested to       |
|                                   |     support previous claims paid  |
|                                   |     and their current claim. See  |
|                                   |     Table 1                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff may need to review previous |
|                                   | claims paid to determine the:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   claim reason,                 |
|                                   | -   claim period, and             |
|                                   | -   relevant dates of information |
|                                   |     to request in the RFI         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer’s claim, select   |
|                                   | [more options] then, Request      |
|                                   | documents.                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Maintain screen in       |
|                                   | Process Direct:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | *Benefit: from the drop down      |
|                                   | menu, select Pandemic Leave       |
|                                   | Disaster Payment                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | *Benefit status: from the drop    |
|                                   | down menu, select New Claim       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Authority to request: from the    |
|                                   | drop down menu, select None – Ex  |
|                                   | Gratia Payment use only           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer required to: from the    |
|                                   | drop down menu, select Upload     |
|                                   | documents or Mail or bring in     |
|                                   | documents, depending on if the    |
|                                   | customer has an online account    |
|                                   | and can access online services    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Request: from the drop down menu, |
|                                   | select 1st                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Information to be supplied: from  |
|                                   | the drop down menu, select 14     |
|                                   | days                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer to contact: from the     |
|                                   | drop down menu, select Call       |
|                                   | Centre                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Invite Reverse Charge Call:       |
|                                   | select No                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Free Text required? select Yes    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Copy and paste the following  |
|                                   |     into the Free Text for Letter |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   |     - If you do not supply all    |
|                                   |     requested evidence by the due |
|                                   |     date your latest claim for    |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment may be rejected and   |
|                                   |     an overpayment may be raised  |
|                                   |     for previously granted        |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claims                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff Notes required? select No   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Available documents               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Search for Other next to the  |
|                                   |     magnifying glass              |
|                                   | -   Select Other                  |
|                                   | -   An Additional Details field   |
|                                   |     will open                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional details                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The RFI letter has 5 free text    |
|                                   | fields. If more than 5 types of   |
|                                   | evidence needs to be requested    |
|                                   | from the customer, add 2 types of |
|                                   | evidence in the one free text     |
|                                   | field so all evidence needed is   |
|                                   | requested in the one letter.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document required for whom:       |
|                                   | select Customer                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Copy and paste the following into |
|                                   | the Free text fields, carefully   |
|                                   | completing the information in the |
|                                   | brackets as per the customer’s    |
|                                   | circumstances. Note: Remove curly |
|                                   | brackets {} and put a full stop   |
|                                   | at the end of each item of        |
|                                   | evidence. This will make sure the |
|                                   | customer can easily read the      |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Free text field 1: If there is no |
|                                   | gap in between the 7 day claiming |
|                                   | periods                           |
|                                   | - Payslips or letter of           |
|                                   | employment or letter of offer or  |
|                                   | contract(s) for employment with   |
|                                   | {ENTER NAME OF THE EMPLOYER} for  |
|                                   | the period {ENTER THE 4 WEEK      |
|                                   | PERIOD BEFORE THE START DATE OF   |
|                                   | THE FIRST 7 DAY CLAIMING PERIOD   |
|                                   | PAID AND ALL PERIODS OF           |
|                                   | SELF-ISOLATION, QUARANTINE OR     |
|                                   | CARING CLAIMED} to show you were  |
|                                   | likely to have worked at least 8  |
|                                   | hours or one full day during the  |
|                                   | periods of self-isolation,        |
|                                   | quarantine or caring claimed      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Free text field 1: If there is a  |
|                                   | gap of 7 days or more in between  |
|                                   | the 7 day claiming periods        |
|                                   | - Payslips or letter of           |
|                                   | employment or letter of offer or  |
|                                   | contract(s) for employment with   |
|                                   | {ENTER NAME OF THE EMPLOYER} for  |
|                                   | the period {ENTER THE 4 WEEK      |
|                                   | PERIOD BEFORE THE START DATE OF   |
|                                   | THE FIRST 7 DAY CLAIMING PERIOD   |
|                                   | PAID AND THE PERIOD BETWEEN OTHER |
|                                   | CLAIMNG PERIODS AND ALL PERIODS   |
|                                   | OF SELF-ISOLATION, QUARANTINE OR  |
|                                   | CARING CLAIMED. IF THERE IS A GAP |
|                                   | IN BETWEEN 7 DAY CLAIMING PERIODS |
|                                   | OF MORE THAN 4 WEEKS, ALSO        |
|                                   | REQUEST EVIDENCE FOR THE 4 WEEKS  |
|                                   | BEFORE THE RELEVANT 7 DAY         |
|                                   | CLAIMING PERIOD} to show you were |
|                                   | likely to have worked at least 8  |
|                                   | hours or one full day during the  |
|                                   | periods of self-isolation,        |
|                                   | quarantine or caring claimed      |
|                                   | - For examples, see Table 5 Step  |
|                                   | 12 in Pandemic Leave Disaster     |
|                                   | Payment                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Note: if the customer is      |
|                                   |     self-employed, request ‘Tax   |
|                                   |     documents, bank statements or |
|                                   |     contract(s) for the period…’  |
|                                   |     instead                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Free text field 2:                |
|                                   | Evidence of all bank balances or  |
|                                   | assets that can be easily         |
|                                   | converted into cash such as money |
|                                   | you may have loaned to another    |
|                                   | person as at {ENTER THE FIRST     |
|                                   | DATE OF THE 7 DAY CLAIMING PERIOD |
|                                   | FOR THE CURRENT CLAIM AND ALL     |
|                                   | CLAIMS PAID WHERE EVIDENCE HAS    |
|                                   | NOT YET BEEN PROVIDED}. Please    |
|                                   | provide bank statements for the   |
|                                   | requested dates.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Free text field 3, 4 and 5: add   |
|                                   | the below depending on the        |
|                                   | customer’s claim reasons          |
|                                   | (tested positive or close         |
|                                   | contact)                          |
|                                   | Evidence of your positive test    |
|                                   | result from a testing centre or   |
|                                   | health professional, or evidence  |
|                                   | you have registered your positive |
|                                   | Rapid Antigen Test result with    |
|                                   | your state or territory health    |
|                                   | authority on {ENTER RELEVANT DATE |
|                                   | DEPENDING ON CLAIM LODGED}. Only  |
|                                   | providing a photo of a positive   |
|                                   | Rapid Antigen Test is not         |
|                                   | sufficient evidence.              |
|                                   | - Evidence of a positive test     |
|                                   | result from a testing centre or   |
|                                   | health professional or evidence   |
|                                   | of a registered positive Rapid    |
|                                   | Antigen Test result with a state  |
|                                   | or territory health authority for |
|                                   | {ENTER NAME OF PERSON THE         |
|                                   | CUSTOMER IS CARING FOR} on {ENTER |
|                                   | RELEVANT DATE DEPENDING ON CLAIM  |
|                                   | LODGED}. Only providing a photo   |
|                                   | of a positive Rapid Antigen Test  |
|                                   | is not sufficient evidence.       |
|                                   | - Medical certificates or letters |
|                                   | from a health professional to     |
|                                   | support all isolation periods     |
|                                   | claimed exceeding 7 days after    |
|                                   | the positive test result on       |
|                                   | {ENTER DATE}. These must state    |
|                                   | you or the person you are caring  |
|                                   | for are still required to isolate |
|                                   | in the period/s claimed due to    |
|                                   | the effects of COVID-19.          |
|                                   | - Evidence of the address and     |
|                                   | positive test result for {ENTER   |
|                                   | NAME/S OF PERSON/S} who has       |
|                                   | tested positive with COVID-19 for |
|                                   | whom you are a close contact.     |
|                                   | Test results must have been       |
|                                   | received from a testing centre or |
|                                   | health professional, or a Rapid   |
|                                   | Antigen Test must have been       |
|                                   | registered with a state or        |
|                                   | territory health authority. Only  |
|                                   | providing a photo of a positive   |
|                                   | Rapid Antigen Test is not         |
|                                   | sufficient evidence.              |
|                                   | - Evidence of the address and     |
|                                   | positive test result for {ENTER   |
|                                   | NAME/S OF PERSON/S} who has       |
|                                   | tested positive with COVID-19 for |
|                                   | whom {ENTER NAME OF PERSON THE    |
|                                   | CUSTOMER IS CARING FOR} is a      |
|                                   | close contact. Test results must  |
|                                   | have been received from a testing |
|                                   | centre or health professional, or |
|                                   | a Rapid Antigen Test must have    |
|                                   | been registered with a state or   |
|                                   | territory health authority. Only  |
|                                   | providing a photo of a positive   |
|                                   | Rapid Antigen Test is not         |
|                                   | sufficient evidence.              |
|                                   | - Evidence that a state or        |
|                                   | territory health official (or an  |
|                                   | authorised contact tracer) has    |
|                                   | advised you, or the person you    |
|                                   | are caring for, are a close       |
|                                   | contact and must isolate.         |
|                                   | - For claims lodged on or after 8 |
|                                   | May 2022 -                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | close contact reasons only        |
|                                   | - Evidence your employer has      |
|                                   | directed you not to attend your   |
|                                   | workplace, even though your state |
|                                   | or territory government does not  |
|                                   | require you to self-isolate       |
|                                   | - Evidence that an educational    |
|                                   | facility has advised the person   |
|                                   | you are caring for must isolate   |
|                                   | - Evidence that a specialist      |
|                                   | school or workplace for a person  |
|                                   | with a disability has advised the |
|                                   | person you are caring for with a  |
|                                   | disability or severe medical      |
|                                   | condition must isolate            |
|                                   | Enter free text here to display   |
|                                   | in the claimant’s online task     |
|                                   | list:                             |
|                                   | - Enter the following:            |
|                                   | Evidence for your Pandemic Leave  |
|                                   | Disaster Payments claim/s is      |
|                                   | required. If you do not supply    |
|                                   | all requested evidence by the due |
|                                   | date, your latest claim for       |
|                                   | Pandemic Leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   | may be rejected and an            |
|                                   | overpayment may be raised for     |
|                                   | previously granted Pandemic Leave |
|                                   | Disaster Payment claims. Required |
|                                   | evidence:                         |
|                                   | - Copy and paste all information  |
|                                   | requested in Free Text Fields 1   |
|                                   | to 5. Note: copying and pasting   |
|                                   | will make sure information in the |
|                                   | free text fields is consistent    |
|                                   | with the claimant’s online task   |
|                                   | list                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Available documents               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Other again            |
|                                   | -   Select >> to move Other under |
|                                   |     Selected Document             |
|                                   | -   Select Finish                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 5                  |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Otherwise, go to Step 7           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Contact attempt + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |
|                                   | Service Officer will call them    |
|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Tell the customer:            |
|                                   |     - you must provide evidence   |
|                                   |     to support this claim and     |
|                                   |     your previous claims. Note:   |
|                                   |     tell the customer what        |
|                                   |     evidence will be requested,   |
|                                   |     depending on their claim      |
|                                   |     reason. See Table 5 Step 12   |
|                                   |     in Pandemic Leave Disaster    |
|                                   |     Payment. Statutory            |
|                                   |     declarations will not be      |
|                                   |     accepted as evidence to       |
|                                   |     support a claim.              |
|                                   |     - you will receive a letter   |
|                                   |     from Services Australia or an |
|                                   |     SMS directing you to complete |
|                                   |     an online task. The letter or |
|                                   |     online task will request that |
|                                   |     you provide this evidence     |
|                                   |     within 14 days of today’s     |
|                                   |     date plus more time as per    |
|                                   |     agency standards otherwise    |
|                                   |     your claim will be ineligible |
|                                   |     - any claims already assessed |
|                                   |     and paid will also be         |
|                                   |     recoverable                   |
|                                   |     - the letter or online task   |
|                                   |     will outline how to provide   |
|                                   |     this evidence                 |
|                                   |     - if you receive a letter     |
|                                   |     please disregard the          |
|                                   |     statement on the letter that  |
|                                   |     reads ‘You can download forms |
|                                   |     to be completed by going to   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   |    servicesaustralia.gov.au/forms |
|                                   |     and searching the name of the |
|                                   |     form’                         |
|                                   |     - Note: if the customer       |
|                                   |     chooses to withdraw their     |
|                                   |     fifth or subsequent claim,    |
|                                   |     tell them they will still     |
|                                   |     need to provide evidence of   |
|                                   |     the previous claims paid      |
|                                   | -   Include in the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note what was discussed |
|                                   |     with the customer             |
|                                   | -   If the customer:              |
|                                   |     - does not withdraw their     |
|                                   |     fifth or subsequent claim, go |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   |     - withdraws their fifth or    |
|                                   |     subsequent claim, go to Step  |
|                                   |     8                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Include in the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note                    |
|                                   |     - that customer contact was   |
|                                   |     attempted, and                |
|                                   |     - why customer contact was    |
|                                   |     needed: ‘To request evidence  |
|                                   |     for PLDP fifth or subsequent  |
|                                   |     claim. Claim ID/s evidence is |
|                                   |     needed for [ENTER CLAIM IDS]’ |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 7                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Correct the ‘OnHold Expiry Date’  |
|                                   | and add keyword + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Request for Information (RFI) |
|                                   | letter will only allow 14 days    |
|                                   | for the return of documents. To   |
|                                   | allow customers time to respond   |
|                                   | as per agency standards, staff    |
|                                   | need to correct the ‘OnHold       |
|                                   | Expiry Date’:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Status icon from the   |
|                                   | menu bar                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select [] to change the status    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Change Status screen will     |
|                                   | show, select On Hold from the     |
|                                   | Status drop down                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Customer to provide    |
|                                   | information as the On Hold Reason |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Set the due to date. For          |
|                                   | customers with:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days + an additional 2        |
|                                   |     working days                  |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days and allow extra time for |
|                                   |     mail delivery, see Time       |
|                                   |     allowed to respond            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the error message ‘OnHold      |
|                                   | Expiry Date’ shows, select the    |
|                                   | third option (current OnHold      |
|                                   | Expiry Date). This will allow the |
|                                   | date nominated in the calendar to |
|                                   | be selected                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If putting a claim back on hold   |
|                                   | as a customer has not been given  |
|                                   | the full number of days requested |
|                                   | to respond, set the due date for  |
|                                   | the remainder of the initial hold |
|                                   | period                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add keyword PHPHRSK               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword ‘PHPHRSK’ in  |
|                                   |     the search field or scroll    |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the PHPHRSK keyword.   |
|                                   |     The keyword will save         |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     the transaction. This will go |
|                                   |     back to the Process Direct    |
|                                   |     Landing Page                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 8.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Add a manual review in Customer   |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Adding a manual review in         |
|                                   | Customer First is an assurance    |
|                                   | measure if the customer:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   decides to withdraw their     |
|                                   |     fifth or subsequent claim     |
|                                   |     while speaking with them, or  |
|                                   | -   withdraws their fifth or      |
|                                   |     subsequent claim later        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This will be a trigger for staff  |
|                                   | to create a minimum standards     |
|                                   | ACTDOC with debt information for  |
|                                   | previous claims paid where the    |
|                                   | customer has:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   withdrawn their fifth or      |
|                                   |     subsequent claim, and/or      |
|                                   | -   not provided the requested    |
|                                   |     evidence to support any       |
|                                   |     claims already paid           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First. Note: staff       |
|                                   | should not have the customer’s    |
|                                   | record open in Customer First and |
|                                   | Process Direct at the same time,  |
|                                   | as this can cause errors.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key ‘RVR’ in the Next field and   |
|                                   | press [Enter] to code a manual    |
|                                   | review on the Review Registration |
|                                   | (RVR) screen:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Reason: select EMG        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review Reason: select Return of   |
|                                   | Correspondence                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Due date: Set the due to date.    |
|                                   | For customers with:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days + an additional 2        |
|                                   |     working days                  |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days + allow extra time for   |
|                                   |     mail delivery, see Time       |
|                                   |     allowed to respond            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source: INT                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: today’s date     |
|                                   | (date letter is sent)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Notes: add the following reason   |
|                                   | for manual review in the free     |
|                                   | text field:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘Evidence requested for PLDP  |
|                                   |     fifth or subsequent claim and |
|                                   |     all previous PLDP claims      |
|                                   |     already granted. If customer  |
|                                   |     withdraws claim see Table 7   |
|                                   |     in OB 003-22011652 for action |
|                                   |     to take. Claim ID/s evidence  |
|                                   |     requested for [ENTER CLAIM    |
|                                   |     IDS]’                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Keyword: PHPHRSK                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Transfer to region: key ‘PDP’     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Press [Enter] or select Continue  |
|                                   | to accept the review.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here, until        |
|                                   | evidence is lodged, or the claim  |
|                                   | or manual review come off hold.   |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | sent to the customer list all     |

|                                   | -   Go to Step 12                 |

|                                   | No,                               |
