+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | Determine next steps based on     |
|                                   | evidence + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not make further contact with  |
|                                   | the customer if they have not     |
|                                   | provided the requested evidence.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Depending on the evidence         |
|                                   | provided by the customer if:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the current and all previous      |
|                                   | claims meet the evidence          |
|                                   | requirements                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If this means the customer    |
|                                   |     will exceed the maximum       |
|                                   |     amount for the event code     |
|                                   |     (that is, if a customer has   |
|                                   |     been paid 6 or more claims    |
|                                   |     for the same event code and   |
|                                   |     is eligible for a seventh of  |
|                                   |     subsequent payment):          |
|                                   |     - do not grant the current    |
|                                   |     claim, as the payment will    |
|                                   |     not issue to the customer due |
|                                   |     to exceeding the maximum      |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   |     - close the customer’s record |
|                                   |     in Customer First to prevent  |
|                                   |     errors                        |
|                                   |     - return to the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   |     - annotate the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section by selecting the      |
|                                   |     Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |     - add details confirming      |
|                                   |     evidence provided and how it  |
|                                   |     was determined the customer   |
|                                   |     was eligible for payment      |
|                                   |     - contact Technical Peer      |
|                                   |     Support who will escalate the |
|                                   |     claim to the Level 2 Helpdesk |
|                                   |     using the Payment Query       |
|                                   |     Template                      |
|                                   |     - go to Table 4               |
|                                   | -   If the customer will not      |
|                                   |     exceed the maximum amount for |
|                                   |     the event code:               |
|                                   |     - close the customer’s record |
|                                   |     in Customer First to prevent  |
|                                   |     errors                        |
|                                   |     - return to the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   |     - to finalise (grant) the     |
|                                   |     current claim go to Table 1   |
|                                   |     Step 34                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the current claim meets the       |
|                                   | evidence requirements but         |
|                                   | previous claims do not            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If this means the customer    |
|                                   |     will exceed the maximum       |
|                                   |     amount for the event code):   |
|                                   |     - do not grant the current    |
|                                   |     claim, as the payment will    |
|                                   |     not issue to the customer due |
|                                   |     to exceeding the maximum      |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   |     - follow the ‘To create the   |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC’     |
|                                   |     steps below to create a       |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC with |
|                                   |     debt information for previous |
|                                   |     claims paid where the         |
|                                   |     requirements were not met     |
|                                   |     - close the customer’s record |
|                                   |     in Customer First to prevent  |
|                                   |     errors                        |
|                                   |     - return to the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   |     - annotate the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note on the DL screen   |
|                                   |     under the Document list/note  |
|                                   |     section by selecting the      |
|                                   |     Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |     - add details confirming      |
|                                   |     evidence provided and how it  |
|                                   |     was determined the customer   |
|                                   |     was eligible for payment      |
|                                   |     - contact Technical Peer      |
|                                   |     Support who will escalate the |
|                                   |     claim to the Level 2 Helpdesk |
|                                   |     using the Payment Query       |
|                                   |     Template                      |
|                                   |     - go to Table 4               |
|                                   | -   If the customer will not      |
|                                   |     exceed the maximum amount for |
|                                   |     the event code:               |
|                                   |     - follow the ‘To create the   |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC’     |
|                                   |     steps below to create a       |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC with |
|                                   |     debt information for previous |
|                                   |     claims paid where the         |
|                                   |     requirements were not met     |
|                                   |     - close the customer’s record |
|                                   |     in Customer First to prevent  |
|                                   |     errors                        |
|                                   |     - return to the customer’s    |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   |     - to finalise (grant) the     |
|                                   |     current claim go to Table 1   |
|                                   |     Step 34                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the current and/or previous       |
|                                   | claims do not meet the evidence   |
|                                   | requirements                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Follow the ‘To create the     |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC’     |
|                                   |     steps below to create a       |
|                                   |     minimum standards ACTDOC with |
|                                   |     debt information for previous |
|                                   |     claims paid where the         |
|                                   |     requirements were not met     |
|                                   | -   Close the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First to stop     |
|                                   |     errors                        |
|                                   | -   Return to the customer’s      |
|                                   |     claim in Process Direct       |
|                                   | -   To finalise (reject) the      |
|                                   |     current claim, go to Table 1  |
|                                   |     Step 34                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | there are concerns about the      |
|                                   | validity of the customer’s        |
|                                   | current claim, previous claims,   |
|                                   | and/or evidence provided, see     |
|                                   | Table 8                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To create the minimum standards   |
|                                   | ACTDOC                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the customer’s record in    |
|                                   | Customer First                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a minimum standards ACTDOC |
|                                   | using the Callback/ACTDOC guided  |
|                                   | procedure                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Search Workspace field     |
|                                   | type: Callback/ACTDOC then select |
|                                   | search                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Click on the Callback/ACTDOC      |
|                                   | hyperlink                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the ACTDOC as follows:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Who contacted: from the drop  |
|                                   |     down select Customer Service  |
|                                   |     Officer                       |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: from the drop |
|                                   |     down select Emergency         |
|                                   |     Exgratia                      |
|                                   | -   Type: from the drop down      |
|                                   |     select ACTDOC                 |
|                                   | -   Category: from the drop down  |
|                                   |     select Debt Raising           |
|                                   | -   Contact Method: from the drop |
|                                   |     down select Internal (to      |
|                                   |     Centrelink)                   |
|                                   | -   Channel: from the drop down   |
|                                   |     select Internal Channels      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Generate Document Content  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Document Content, add the      |
|                                   | reason the customer was overpaid. |
|                                   | Include the details of how the    |
|                                   | overpayment occurred, such as:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   customer did not provide the  |
|                                   |     requested evidence to support |
|                                   |     the payment of a {ENTER CLAIM |
|                                   |     NUMBER, for example, fifth    |
|                                   |     claim, sixth claim} for       |
|                                   |     {ENTER CLAIM ID}. {ENTER      |
|                                   |     NUMBER OF CLAIMS ALREADY      |
|                                   |     PAID, for example, 4 claims,  |
|                                   |     5 claims} have already been   |
|                                   |     paid for the following CLAIM  |
|                                   |     IDs {ENTER CLAIM IDs PAID}.   |
|                                   |     Overpayment to be raised for  |
|                                   |     all previous claims paid for  |
|                                   |     self-isolation, quarantine or |
|                                   |     caring periods that start on  |
|                                   |     or after 18 January 2022      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Finish at the top left     |
|                                   | corner of the screen              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Activity List (AL)      |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the ACTDOC activity        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select O Transfer the activity to |
|                                   | another site or region            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Regional Office enter: XWA     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In New Keywords add keyword:      |
|                                   | PLDPDEBT                          |

Reporting potential fraud

Table 8

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Report suspected fraud + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff should report suspected     |
|                                   | fraud if they:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   have concerns about the       |
|                                   |     identity of a person making a |
|                                   |     claim, or                     |
|                                   | -   suspect the customer is       |
|                                   |     acting fraudulently when      |
|                                   |     claiming the Pandemic Leave   |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Important points when reporting   |
|                                   | suspected fraud:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   do not investigate the record |
|                                   |     any further than is needed to |
|                                   |     complete regular duties       |
|                                   | -   do not search the system for  |
|                                   |     customer information in order |
|                                   |     to complete the report        |
|                                   | -   only provide details in the   |
|                                   |     report that were received or  |
|                                   |     became apparent during the    |
|                                   |     interaction with the customer |
|                                   |     or processing of the claim    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not grant the claim.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 2.                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Record DOA DOC in Customer        |
|                                   | First + Read more ...             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Home button at the top |
|                                   | left hand side to exit out of the |
|                                   | transaction and the customer’s    |
|                                   | record. This will return to the   |
|                                   | Process Direct landing page.      |
|                                   | Pending DOA DOC functionality in  |
|                                   | Process Direct, access the        |
|                                   | customer’s record in Customer     |
|                                   | First to add a Display on Access  |
|                                   | (DOA) DOC. Any future claims      |
|                                   | lodged by the customer will not   |
|                                   | meet the rules for straight       |
|                                   | through processing.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To create the DOA DOC in Customer |
|                                   | First run the Fast Note workflow: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Search Workspace: Key Fast     |
|                                   | Note then select Search           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Fast Note hyperlink    |
|                                   | and complete the Fast Note        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Who contacted: From the drop down |
|                                   | box select CSO Customer Service   |
|                                   | Officer                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: From the drop |
|                                   |     down box select the           |
|                                   |     following:                    |
|                                   | -   select EXG - Emergency        |
|                                   |     Ex-gratia                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: Date DOC created |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Channel: From the drop down box   |
|                                   | select INT- Internal Channels     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source: From the drop down select |
|                                   | INT-Internal                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Auto text. From the drop   |
|                                   | down box select:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Category 1: Emergency         |
|                                   | -   Category 2: Claim             |
|                                   | -   Template: Caution for         |
|                                   |     Emergency Pymts               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Display on Access          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Confirm                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DOA reason screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reason: Auto populates to SCC     |
|                                   | -Special Contact Considerations   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Expiry Date: auto populates   |
|                                   | -   Select Confirm                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Answer all questions/prompts      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For a DOA DOC about false         |
|                                   | evidence uploaded, include:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim for the Pandemic Leave  |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment should not   |
|                                   |     be granted for this customer  |
|                                   |     If the customer contacts      |
|                                   |     about the status of their     |
|                                   |     claim, staff can tell them    |
|                                   |     'the evidence uploaded does   |
|                                   |     not support your claim, so    |
|                                   |     your claim cannot be granted  |
|                                   |     as eligibility cannot be      |
|                                   |     established                   |
|                                   |     False evidence has been       |
|                                   |     reported                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For a DOA DOC about identity or   |
|                                   | claim details, include:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim for Pandemic Leave      |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment should not   |
|                                   |     be granted for this customer  |
|                                   |     unless documentary evidence   |
|                                   |     is provided                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer contacts about    |
|                                   | the status of their claim, staff  |
|                                   | can tell them the following as    |
|                                   | appropriate:                      |
|                                   | - ‘Your identity could not be     |
|                                   | confirmed. Additional proof of    |
|                                   | identity documents must be        |
|                                   | provided for the claim to be      |
|                                   | assessed, or your claim cannot be |
|                                   | granted, as identity cannot be    |
|                                   | established’                      |
|                                   | - ‘Evidence to support your claim |
|                                   | must be provided for the claim to |
|                                   | be assessed, or your claim cannot |
|                                   | be granted, as eligibility cannot |
|                                   | be established’                   |
|                                   | - ‘Validity of identity/claims    |
|                                   | made has been referred’           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not use the term ‘fraud’   |
|                                   |     in the DOA DOC or if speaking |
|                                   |     with a customer               |
|                                   | -   Consider if a minimum         |
|                                   |     standards ACTDOC with debt    |
|                                   |     information for previous      |
|                                   |     claims paid is needed         |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 3                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Annotate the Note in Process      |
|                                   | Direct + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Close the customer's record in    |
|                                   | Customer first. Return to the     |
|                                   | customer's claim in Process       |
|                                   | Direct.                           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | already been done).               |

|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer advised they  |
|                                   |     will provide evidence to      |
|                                   |     support their claim, do not   |
|                                   |     reject the claim yet.         |
|                                   |     Procedure ends here until     |
|                                   |     evidence is provided or the   |
|                                   |     claim comes of hold. Then go  |
|                                   |     to Table 3 Step 7             |
|                                   | -   Otherwise, reject the claim   |

Cancelled JobSeeker Payment or Youth Allowance

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 9: if a customer has:

-   voluntarily cancelled their JobSeeker Payment (JSP) or Youth
    Allowance (YA) in the 28 days before the start date of the 7 day
    period they are claiming the Pandemic leave Disaster Payment, and
-   has not reported employment or self-employment income in their last
    payment period

This would have been identified in Table 1.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Requesting evidence or claim has  |
|                                   | come off hold + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: statutory declarations will |
|                                   | not be accepted as evidence to    |
|                                   | support a claim.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If evidence to support the        |
|                                   | customer would have worked in the |
|                                   | 7 day period they are claiming    |
|                                   | the Pandemic leave Disaster       |
|                                   | Payment (including                |
|                                   | self-employment income) has       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | not yet been requested, go to     |
|                                   | Step 2                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | been requested and staff have     |
|                                   | been allocated a work item that   |
|                                   | has come off hold. If the hold    |
|                                   | period ending is                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   due to a request for          |
|                                   |     information ending, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 8                        |
|                                   | -   not due to a request for      |
|                                   |     information ending            |
|                                   |     - Check the claim to          |
|                                   |     determine if any updates or   |
|                                   |     actions are needed            |
|                                   |     - If the claim cannot be      |
|                                   |     finalised as the customer has |
|                                   |     not been provided 14 days to  |
|                                   |     respond, plus more time as    |
|                                   |     per agency standards, place   |
|                                   |     the claim on hold again for   |
|                                   |     the remainder of the initial  |
|                                   |     hold period. For example, if  |
|                                   |     a customer was given 22 days  |
|                                   |     to respond and only 2 days    |
|                                   |     have passed since the request |
|                                   |     for information was made,     |
|                                   |     hold the claim for a further  |
|                                   |     20 days. To hold the claim,   |
|                                   |     go to Step 7                  |
|                                   |     - If the claim can be         |
|                                   |     finalised as the customer has |
|                                   |     been provided 14 days to      |
|                                   |     respond, plus more time as    |
|                                   |     per agency standards, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 8                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | been requested and staff identify |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the review date for the       |
|                                   |     Request for Information (RFI) |
|                                   |     letter sent has expired, and  |
|                                   | -   no action has been taken to   |
|                                   |     determine next steps,         |
|                                   |     - Go to Step 8                |

| 2                                 | Check if claim was lodged using   |
|                                   | Assisted Customer Claim (ACC) and |

|                                   | Information (RFI) will be sent +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | screen, if the ‘Channel’ of the   |
|                                   | claim shows as:                   |

|                                   | WEB CHANNEL, this is an online    |
|                                   | claim lodged by a customer        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ‘Submitted by’ will show the  |
|                                   |     customer’s CRN                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | INTERNAL this is a phone claim    |
|                                   | lodged using ACC                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim shows as INTERNAL,   |
|                                   | key ‘DL‘ in the Super Key field   |
|                                   | to go the customer’s Document     |
|                                   | List (DL) screen.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there a DOC titled PLDP claim  |
|                                   | JSP/YAL CLR that relates to the   |
|                                   | customers claim? Note: this DOC   |
|                                   | should have been created where    |
|                                   | required during a phone claim     |
|                                   | (Assisted Customer Claim).        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, customer contact is not      |
|                                   | needed, as this DOC means the     |
|                                   | customer:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   lodged a phone claim          |

| 4                                 | Contact attempt + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is subscribed,    |
|                                   | issue a pre-call notification     |
|                                   | (SMS only) between 8:00 am and    |
|                                   | 8:00 pm using the customer's      |
|                                   | local time, to let them know a    |

|                                   | today from a private number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make one genuine attempt to       |
|                                   | contact the customer.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the contact successful?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer does not wish |
|                                   |     to proceed with their         |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment claim and decides to  |
|                                   |     restore their JSP or YA       |
|                                   |     - Encourage the customer to   |
|                                   |     withdraw their claim,         |
|                                   |     otherwise it will be          |
|                                   |     ineligible.                   |
|                                   |     - If trained in JSP or YA,    |
|                                   |     help the customer.            |
|                                   |     - If not trained in JSP or YA |
|                                   |     complete an unannounced       |
|                                   |     (cold) transfer to the        |
|                                   |     Employment Services queue in  |
|                                   |     Services Australia Workspace. |
|                                   |     - Include in the Progress of  |
|                                   |     Claim Note what was discussed |
|                                   |     with the customer             |
|                                   |     - Procedure ends here.        |
|                                   | -   If the customer wishes to     |
|                                   |     proceed with their Pandemic   |
|                                   |     Leave Disaster Payment claim, |
|                                   |     tell the customer:            |
|                                   |     - You must provide evidence   |
|                                   |     that you would have earned    |
|                                   |     employment or self-employment |
|                                   |     income in the 7 day period    |
|                                   |     you are claiming the Pandemic |
|                                   |     Leave Disaster Payment.       |
|                                   |     Statutory declarations will   |
|                                   |     not be accepted as evidence   |
|                                   |     to support a claim            |
|                                   |     - Evidence may include        |
|                                   |     payslips or bank statements   |
|                                   |     - For customers who are       |
|                                   |     self-employed, evidence may   |
|                                   |     include bank statements,      |
|                                   |     contracts or invoices. Note:  |
|                                   |     there is no specific question |
|                                   |     in the Pandemic Leave         |
|                                   |     Disaster Payment online claim |
|                                   |     that asks the customer if     |
|                                   |     they are self-employed. Staff |
|                                   |     can identify this where the   |
|                                   |     customer’s name (and possibly |
|                                   |     address) are the same as the  |
|                                   |     employment details provided   |
|                                   |     in their claim                |
|                                   |     - You will receive a letter   |
|                                   |     from Services Australia or an |
|                                   |     SMS directing you to complete |
|                                   |     an online task. The letter or |
|                                   |     online task will request that |
|                                   |     you provide this evidence     |
|                                   |     within 14 days of today’s     |
|                                   |     date plus more time as per    |
|                                   |     agency standards otherwise    |
|                                   |     your claim will be ineligible |
|                                   |     - The letter or online task   |
|                                   |     will outline how to provide   |
|                                   |     this evidence                 |
|                                   |     - If you receive a letter     |
|                                   |     please disregard the          |
|                                   |     statement on the letter that  |
|                                   |     reads ‘You can download forms |
|                                   |     to be completed by going to   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   |    servicesaustralia.gov.au/forms |
|                                   |     and searching the name of the |
|                                   |     form’                         |
|                                   | -   If the customer advises they  |
|                                   |     do not have the required      |
|                                   |     evidence, tell them           |
|                                   |     - Your claim does not meet    |
|                                   |     the requirements for payment  |
|                                   |     - You will receive a letter   |
|                                   |     that your claim is ineligible |
|                                   | -   Include in the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note what was discussed |
|                                   |     with the customer             |
|                                   | -   If the customer advises they: |
|                                   |     - have the evidence needed to |
|                                   |     support their claim, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   |     - do not have the evidence    |
|                                   |     needed to support their       |
|                                   |     claim, go to Table 1 Step 34  |
|                                   |     to finalise (reject) the      |
|                                   |     claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Include in the Progress of    |
|                                   |     Claim Note                    |
|                                   |     - that customer contact was   |
|                                   |     attempted, and                |
|                                   |     - why customer contact was    |
|                                   |     needed                        |
|                                   | -   No further customer contact   |
|                                   |     is needed.                    |
|                                   | -   Go to Table 1 Step 34 to      |
|                                   |     finalise (reject) the claim.  |

| 5                                 | Send RFI + Read more ...          |

|                                   |     - If you do not supply all    |
|                                   |     requested evidence by the due |
|                                   |     date your latest claim for    |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Disaster       |
|                                   |     Payment may be rejected       |
|                                   | -   Staff Notes required? select  |
|                                   |     No                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Available documents               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Search for Other next to the  |
|                                   |     magnifying glass              |
|                                   | -   Select Other                  |
|                                   | -   An Additional Details field   |
|                                   |     will open                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional details                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document required for whom:       |
|                                   | select Customer                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Copy and paste the following into |
|                                   | the Free text field 1             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Evidence that you would have  |
|                                   |     earned employment or          |
|                                   |     self-employment income in the |
|                                   |     7 day period you are claiming |
|                                   |     the Pandemic leave Disaster   |
|                                   |     Payment. Examples of evidence |
|                                   |     includes payslips, bank       |
|                                   |     statements, contracts and     |
|                                   |     invoices (if you are          |
|                                   |     self-employed)                |
|                                   | -   Enter free text here to       |
|                                   |     display in the claimant’s     |
|                                   |     online task list: copy and    |
|                                   |     paste the information         |
|                                   |     requested in Free Text Field  |
|                                   |     1. Note: copying and pasting  |
|                                   |     will make sure information in |
|                                   |     the free text field is        |
|                                   |     consistent with the           |
|                                   |     claimant’s online task list.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Available documents               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Other again            |
|                                   | -   Select >> to move Other under |
|                                   |     Selected Document             |
|                                   | -   Select Finish                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 6                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Annotate Progress of Claim Note + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Notes icon from the    |
|                                   | menu bar, then annotate the       |
|                                   | Progress of Claim Note on the DL  |
|                                   | screen under the Document         |
|                                   | list/note section by selecting    |
|                                   | the Annotate hyperlink            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Clearly document:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   why the claim cannot be       |
|                                   |     finalised                     |
|                                   | -   what information was          |
|                                   |     requested in the RFI          |
|                                   | -   the claim IDs evidence was    |
|                                   |     requested for                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 7                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Correct the ‘OnHold Expiry Date’  |
|                                   | and add keyword + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Request for Information (RFI) |
|                                   | letter will only allow 14 days    |
|                                   | for the return of documents. To   |
|                                   | allow customers time to respond   |
|                                   | as per agency standards, staff    |
|                                   | need to correct the ‘On Hold      |
|                                   | Expiry Date’:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Status icon from the   |
|                                   | menu bar                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select [] to change the status    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Change Status screen will     |
|                                   | show, select On Hold from the     |
|                                   | Status drop down                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Customer to provide    |
|                                   | information as the On Hold Reason |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Set the due to date. For          |
|                                   | customers with:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   an online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days + an additional 2        |
|                                   |     working days                  |
|                                   | -   no online account, select a   |
|                                   |     date from the calendar 14     |
|                                   |     days and allow extra time for |
|                                   |     mail delivery, see Time       |
|                                   |     allowed to respond            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the error message ‘OnHold      |
|                                   | Expiry Date’ shows, select the    |
|                                   | third option (current On Hold     |
|                                   | Expiry Date). This will allow the |
|                                   | date nominated in the calendar to |
|                                   | be selected                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If putting a claim back on hold   |
|                                   | as a customer has not been given  |
|                                   | the full number of days requested |
|                                   | to respond, set the due date for  |
|                                   | the remainder of the initial hold |
|                                   | period                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Save                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add keyword PHPHRSK               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Keyword icon from  |
|                                   |     the menu bar                  |
|                                   | -   Select the Add (+) icon       |
|                                   | -   Key the keyword ‘PHPHRSK’ in  |
|                                   |     the search field or scroll    |
|                                   |     through the list to find it   |
|                                   | -   Select the PHPHRSK keyword.   |
|                                   |     The keyword will save         |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     the transaction. This will go |
|                                   |     back to the Process Direct    |
|                                   |     Landing Page                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here, until        |
|                                   | evidence is lodged, or the claim  |
|                                   | comes off hold.                   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Allocated a claim in Process      |
|                                   | Direct that has come off hold or  |
|                                   | review date of RFI has expired +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key ‘DL’ in the Super Key field   |
|                                   | to go the customer’s Document     |
|                                   | List (DL) screen                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Check if the customer has         |
|                                   | provided evidence they would have |
|                                   | earned employment or              |
|                                   | self-employment income in the 7   |
|                                   | day period they are claiming the  |
|                                   | Pandemic leave Disaster Payment   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Review any RFI letters sent   |
|                                   |     to the customer to make sure  |
|                                   |     the required evidence has     |
|                                   |     been requested                |
|                                   | -   To review RFI letters:        |
|                                   |     - key HS in the Super Key     |
|                                   |     field to go to the History    |
|                                   |     Summary (HS) screen           |
|                                   |     - select the relevant PDF.    |
|                                   |     Note: if the HS screen shows  |
|                                   |     an SMS notification only,     |
|                                   |     check the Tasks icon in the   |
|                                   |     claim to see what information |
|                                   |     the customer has been asked   |
|                                   |     to provide in an ‘online      |
|                                   |     task’                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has an RFI been sent requesting   |
|                                   | the required evidence?            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, and the customer has         |
|                                   | provided evidence that supports   |
|                                   | their claim                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Check the claim to make sure  |
|                                   |     the customer meets all        |
|                                   |     eligibility criteria          |
|                                   | -   Go to Table 1 Step 34 to      |
|                                   |     finalise (grant or reject)    |
|                                   |     the claim                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, and the customer has not     |
|                                   | provided the requested evidence,  |
|                                   | or evidence provided by the       |
|                                   | customer does not support their   |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Table 1 Step 34 to      |
|                                   |     finalise (reject) the claim   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Request the evidence. See     |
|                                   |     Table 9 Step 1                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

POIPLDP manual review allocated

Do not follow this procedure for self-isolation, quarantine or caring
periods that start on or before 17 January 2022. See Processing Pandemic
Leave Disaster Payment Claims in Customer First.

Table 10: if staff are allocated a manual review with the keyword
POIPLDP.

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Manual review allocated + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When a customer lodges an         |
|                                   | Assisted Customer Claim (ACC),    |
|                                   | they are asked to provide the     |
|                                   | details of identity documents to  |
|                                   | be verified in the Identity       |
|                                   | Confirmation Dashboard in process |
|                                   | Direct before the ACC is run. See |
|                                   | Table 3 in Pandemic Leave         |
|                                   | Disaster Payment - Assisted       |
|                                   | Customer Claims.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the identity documents do not  |
|                                   | verify, an Alternative Identity   |
|                                   | Assessment is completed. This     |
|                                   | assessment may tell the customer  |
|                                   | the actions they need to take in  |
|                                   | a specified timeframe, otherwise  |
|                                   | their payment may be cancelled.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The timeframe specified is as per |
|                                   | the Alternative identity category |
|                                   | shown in the Identity             |
|                                   | Confirmation Dashboard.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff taking the ACC need to      |
|                                   | create a manual review in         |
|                                   | Customer First with the keyword   |
|                                   | POIPLDP.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If staff are allocated a manual   |
|                                   | review with the keyword POIPLDP   |
|                                   | they need to check one document   |
|                                   | from each category below has been |
|                                   | coded in the Identity             |
|                                   | Confirmation Dashboard:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Commencement of Identity (CoI)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A customer can demonstrate    |
|                                   |     CoI in Australia by providing |
|                                   |     documents that confirm their  |
|                                   |     birth in Australia or proof   |
|                                   |     of arrival in Australia,      |
|                                   |     establishing the customer's   |
|                                   |     existence in Australia        |
|                                   | -   If a customer cannot provide  |
|                                   |     a CoI document, see           |
|                                   |     Commencement of Identity      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Primary Use in Community (PUiC)   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   These documents are generally |
|                                   |     government issued and most    |
|                                   |     have a photograph and         |
|                                   |     security features             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Secondary Use in Community (SUiC) |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   These documents can be        |
|                                   |     government or non-government  |
|                                   |     issued and show use of        |
|                                   |     identity in the community     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To check this, close the          |
|                                   | customer’s record in Customer     |
|                                   | First.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: staff should not have the   |
|                                   | customer’s record open in         |
|                                   | Customer First and Process Direct |
|                                   | at the same time, as this can     |
|                                   | cause errors.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer’s record in       |
|                                   | Process Direct:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Identity Confirmation  |
|                                   |     from the Task Selector        |
|                                   | -   Select Start to open the      |
|                                   |     Identity Confirmation         |
|                                   |     Dashboard                     |
|                                   | -   Check if the customer has got |
|                                   |     a CoI, PUiC and SUiC document |
|                                   |     verified                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a COI,     |
|                                   | PUiC and SUiC document verified?  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Table 5 Step 3      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Finalise the manual review + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key ‘DL’ in the Super Key     |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   | -   Annotate all relevant         |
|                                   |     Pandemic Leave Claim - Grant  |
|                                   |     Summary Notes by selecting    |
|                                   |     the Annotate hyperlink        |
|                                   | -   Record that the customer has  |
|                                   |     provided the required         |
|                                   |     identity documents in the     |
|                                   |     specified timeframe           |
|                                   | -   Select Save                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Home button at the |
|                                   |     top left hand side to exit    |
|                                   |     out of the transaction and    |
|                                   |     the customer’s record. Note:  |
|                                   |     staff should not have the     |
|                                   |     customer’s record open in     |
|                                   |     Customer First and Process    |
|                                   |     Direct at the same time, as   |
|                                   |     this can cause errors.        |
|                                   | -   Go to the customer’s record   |
|                                   |     in Customer First             |
|                                   | -   Key AL in the Next field and  |
|                                   |     press [Enter]                 |
|                                   | -   Select the manual review with |
|                                   |     the keyword POIPLDP           |
|                                   | -   Select cancel and continue    |
|                                   | -   Select Yes - cancel the       |
|                                   |     Activity and continue         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
